Matsuoka Passes Through Moscow　Soviet Telegram 61

The relations between the Soviet Union and Japan are sometimes clear and bright, sometimes gloomy, sometimes approaching and friendly, and sometimes deploying troops and generals as if facing a formidable enemy. Although the reporter also lives in the cold and barren red zone, he still cannot see clearly whether their true intention is to join eyebrows and fight it out (?), or to conclude a Soviet-Japanese non-aggression treaty to ease the current tense situation (?).

Logically speaking, Japan is an empire, although it hangs the sign of constitutionalism, it is actually a military dictatorship. Especially in the past year, the military's arrogance has been rampant. Deploying troops to the three northeastern provinces has not only trampled on China's regime in the Northeast with iron hooves, crushed the 30 million people of China, but also trampled on the Soviet Union's rights in northern Manchuria, including the Chinese Eastern Railway. Moreover, the Japanese military has also shattered his parliamentary politics with an iron fist. Everyone knows that the Soviet Union is a dictatorial country ruled by the Communist Party, but it is a country moving towards socialism. Although it may not be able to fully realize its ideals at present, its planned future and its current actions are different from other countries, especially from Japan, which are truly incompatible like ice and charcoal. However, there are also two different views on Japan in the Soviet Union. One is that the current People's Commissar for the Army and Navy, Voroshilov, advocates prudence and first strengthening one's own strength. The commander of the Far Eastern Army, Blucher (i.e., former Galen General who served as an advisor to the National Revolutionary Army), believes that if Japan is too aggressive, it should respond without any tolerance.

After Japan occupied Manchuria, it not only concluded a military alliance with Manchuria but also became one with Manchuria, transforming Manchuria into Japan's vanguard. Japan and Manchuria became the same military unit. At the same time, economically, it also wants to create the so-called Japanese-Manchurian economic alliance. In terms of external significance, whether in military or economic aspects, it contains a deep intention to be hostile to the Soviet Union. Of course, on the other hand, it is also a base for war against the United States. However, what Japan is most uneasy about and also most embarrassing in Manchuria is a long sword inserted into the belly of northern Manchuria, the Chinese Eastern Railway. This railway runs straight through the two provinces of Heilongjiang and Jilin. Under the current situation, not only does it have close relations with Manchuria, but in terms of Japan's vested interests in Manchuria, it is at least a very large cancer, which is enough to make Manchuria's puppet unstable and enough to fundamentally shake the continental policy of Japanese imperialism. Therefore, Japan, on the one hand, uses diplomatic tactics to hint to Britain and France that Japan is the vanguard of the East standing on the front line of defending against Russia. Japan's seizure of "Manchuria" is for the so-called peace. However, at the same time, he also knows that the League of Nations is a tool of Britain and France. Now that Germany is unruly and Italy is allied with Germany, France's hegemony in Europe is about to be fundamentally shaken. Therefore, France cannot but find ways to maintain the face of the League of Nations. Thus, some restrictions had to be placed on Japan.

In order to maintain what it had gained through aggression and to resist the great powers from interfering in "Manchuria", Japan could not but temporarily try to win over the Soviet Union and use the Soviet Union as its diplomatic tool.

The Soviet Union itself knows very well that its industry is more backward than several strong capitalist countries. To create a socialist country in a capitalist environment, it must go through considerable hard work. Therefore, the implementation of the New Economic Policy and the first and second Five-Year Plans both focus on their own basic work, mechanization and electrification.

Page 6

化││At this time, it will never provoke any trouble with the outside world.

The Japanese military initially did not understand the Soviet Union's intention, so it was quite wary of the Soviet Union's active preparations. Recently, it gradually understood that the Far Eastern Army was "preparing for defense and war."

The End of Traitors 62

Cheng Zhiyuan Executed by Firing Squad

Zhao Zhongren Detained

According to a certain source, Cheng Zhiyuan, the puppet acting governor of Heilongjiang Province, was originally the commander of the Heilongjiang Garrison. After the Japanese arrived, they were quite suspicious of Cheng. They once transferred Cheng to Changchun to serve as a puppet national military advisor. The position of commander of the Heilongjiang Garrison was given to Zhang Wenzhu. When Su Bingwen's National Salvation Army rose up, the Japanese ordered Cheng to command Zhang's army to attack the National Salvation Army. Although Zhang's army was Cheng's old unit, upon hearing that they were attacking Su, they disobeyed Cheng's orders and the troops could not depart. The Japanese then dismissed their suspicions and reassigned Cheng. At the time, the commander of the Japanese Second Division, Tamon Jirō, detained Cheng in Heihe and then executed him by firing squad. This happened around late last month. Furthermore, Zhao Zhongren, the puppet provincial committee member and finance director of Heilongjiang, was also recently detained by Tamon in Heihe. Originally, the Japanese knew that Zhao was acquainted with Su Bingwen and sent him to Hailar to persuade Su. Zhao obeyed the order and went, but was severely rebuked by Su and returned. The Japanese side blamed him for failing to complete his mission, so they detained him. Zhao was in his forties and the richest man in Heilongjiang. He privately operated a small-scale railway between Ang'angxi and Qiqihar, so his wealth can be imagined. Last year, he introduced Japanese staff officer Itagaki to Ma Zhanshan in Ma's army, acting as an intermediary. It can be seen that he had long decided to be a slave. Although the Japanese utilized such people, they also greatly despised them. Therefore, if these people were no longer beneficial to Japan, they would gradually be eliminated by various means. Cheng and Zhao were probably among them. It is rumored that after Zhao was detained, a portion of his property was confiscated by the Japanese. However, it is still unknown whether his life is in danger.

However, the true intention of the Moscow government is to observe the Far Eastern situation with an attitude of "static observation". Japan took this opportunity to win over the Soviet Union. The past performance of this is that Japan has received considerable gains in both the fishery agreement and the oil agreement.

Politically, in this tense period, what methods did Japan use? Matsuoka Yōsuke, on his way to Geneva, stopped in Moscow on his way through Siberia for a short stay.

He first paid a visit to Deputy Foreign Minister Karakhan, then went to see Foreign Affairs People's Commissar Litvinov, and then visited Molotov, even going so far as to pay his respects to Stalin, the authority of the Communist Party. And in order to show cordiality, he did not hesitate to participate in the Red Memorial Day (November 7th), which the "Empire" most feared and dreaded. Matsuoka's meeting with the general authorities of the Soviet Union can be roughly divided into the following points:

1. A non-aggression treaty between the Soviet Union and Japan must have conditions for exchange. Matsuoka, in the red atmosphere, did not dare to be too explicit, saying that he wanted the Northern Sea fishery, the Siberian forest and mineral resources, and could only describe Japan's intention to be friendly and that Japan and the Soviet Union should mutually understand and jointly maintain the current situation in "Manchukuo."

2. To inquire whether the Soviet Union is willing to immediately recognize the "Manchukuo (puppet) state" established by Japan.

3. Regarding the China Eastern Railway, although Japan plans to cut it off, it is ultimately a disease of the abdomen. Matsuoka's intention was to explore whether the Soviet Union could sell the China Eastern Railway to Japan and expressed Japan's willingness to pay a considerable price.

The Soviet authorities' reply was very interesting, saying, "Since the outbreak of the Sino-Japanese conflict, the Soviet Union has maintained its desire for peace and adhered to neutrality... As for other issues (apart from the non-aggression treaty, which can be discussed), we have not prepared to consider them..."

The smooth and sophisticated Matsuoka encountered such a red "elephant skin nail" in Moscow, and left by train to the west with disappointment (November 20, 1932, in Vladivostok).

Japan Expands Naval Force to Threaten America 63

Participating in Next Year's Grand Exercises Plan

Content of the Newly Formed Three Major Fleets

According to the Nagoya Shimbun of Japan, a Tokyo dispatch states that the Navy has decided to hold grand exercises on an extremely wide scale in the coming year, and has increased funding by one million to five million yen in the next year's budget. The plan for the grand exercises is as follows: Selecting the southern Pacific Ocean off Honshu, Japan as the site. The participating units will include the Combined Fleet newly formed on December 1st, the four battleships Hyūga, Mutsu, Haruna, and Kongō, as well as the new 10,000-ton cruisers Atago, Chōkai, Takao, and Maya, which previously participated in the grand exercises, and will also include the cruisers and aircraft carrier Ryūjō. The combined reserve fleets of hundreds of ships will be distributed, and all aircraft of the naval air force will be mobilized at the same time. The Yokosuka, Kure, Sasebo, and the three guard districts, as well as various important port units, will be fully mobilized to concentrate the new scientific essence of the sea and air to hold a grand naval battle exercise. After the grand exercise, a naval review will be held outside Yokosuka Port.

Naval Minister Okada, with the approval of the Emperor on the first of this month, formed fleets as follows: A. The 1st Fleet: The 1st Squadron includes four battleships: Kongō, Hyūga, Mutsu, and Haruna. The 2nd Squadron includes Abukuma, Yura, and Natori. The 1st Torpedo Squadron includes Jintsū and the 28th and 30th Submarine Squadrons. B. The 2nd Fleet: The 4th Squadron includes Takao, Atago, Maya, and Chōkai. The 5th Squadron includes Kinugasa, Kako, and Aoba. The 2nd Torpedo Squadron includes Naka, the 7th, 8th, 11th, and 12th Destroyer Squadrons. Attached to the Combined Fleet are Mamiya, Naruto, Tsurumi, and Notoro. The 1st Overseas Fleet includes Tsushima, Ataka, Uji, Sumida, Fushimi, Seta, Katada, Hira, Hozu, Atami, Futami, Urakaze, and the 24th Destroyer Squadron. The 3rd Overseas Fleet includes Hirado and the 16th Destroyer Squadron. The Training Fleet includes Yakumo and Kasagi. C. The 3rd Fleet includes Izumo, Tenryū, and the 27th Destroyer Squadron.

Reorganization of Guangdong and Guangxi Air Forces 64

Guangdong Deploys Two Wings, Six Squadrons

Guangxi Deploys Three Teams with Eighteen Aircraft

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the Guangdong Provincial Air Force Headquarters moved to Shougouling in the eastern suburbs, all aircraft have also been moved there. Recently, due to the continuous addition of fighter planes, it is necessary to have a large number of hangars to store them. The hangars at Dashatou were dismantled and new hangars were built at Shougouling. As for the personnel of each squadron, they have also been engaged in screening recently. A flight technology examination committee was specially formed by the Air Force Headquarters to examine the pilots of each squadron. The first and second squadrons have been examined. Last week, the Air Force Department also sent Lin Fuyuan, the chief of staff of the department, to Shaoguan to personally examine the pilots of the third aircraft squadron stationed in Shaoguan. After the examination of the members of each squadron, they began to reorganize all the pilots. The new reorganization plan was approved by the First Army Group Headquarters on the 25th. On the 26th, the Air Force Department held a meeting to discuss the reorganization and decided to establish the reorganization and the oath of office ceremony for the newly appointed officers next month (December) on the 15th. The new organization includes two large squadrons, each squadron governing three squadrons. The designated squadron leaders are: Tan Shou, the leader of the first squadron; Ding Jixu, the leader of the second squadron; Tao Zuode, the leader of the first squadron; Ma Tinghuai, the leader of the second squadron; Ao Lun, the leader of the third squadron; Xie Mang, the leader of the fourth squadron; Wu Jianwen, the leader of the fifth squadron; and Qiu Wenlin, the leader of the sixth squadron. This is the situation of the recent deployment of the Guangdong aircraft squadron. As for Guangxi Province, Bai Chongxi has also been actively expanding the air force recently. Initially, personnel were borrowed from Guangdong to establish a civil aviation bureau in Guilin to train Guangxi pilots. The flight organization was roughly established. Recently, the purchase of aircraft has been changed to the Aviation Office, which is subordinate to the Fourth Army Group Headquarters. Since then, it has changed from civil to military use. Guangxi Province has purchased a total of eighteen aircraft and compiled them into three aircraft teams, regardless of the name of the large squadron. Each team is equipped with six aircraft, with Lin Weicheng as the director of the Aviation Office. Ning Mingjie, Wu Zihong, and Wu Ruliu serve as the captains of the first, second, and third teams respectively. Xu Shiying is the director of the training class of the Aviation Office. Recently, the Aviation Office was moved to Liuzhou to establish it (November 28th).

Hindenburg Formally Appoints Schleicher Cabinet 65

National Socialist Party and Communist Party Express No Support

Political Circles Hope for a Compromise Solution

Reuters, Berlin, 3rd: New Prime Minister Schleicher has largely determined the distribution of cabinet members. Schleicher will continue to serve concurrently as Minister of Defense, Neurath will continue as Minister of Foreign Affairs, Gayl as Minister of Interior, and Schwerin von Krosigk as Minister of Finance. The remaining distributions have also been compromised, but the Ministry of Economy and the Ministry of Agriculture have not yet been decided. The new cabinet members have been approved by President Hindenburg and have already held their first cabinet meeting. The Reichstag is scheduled to convene on Tuesday and will adjourn after a few days until after Christmas in order to facilitate discussions among the parties on future procedures to obtain greater agreement.

▲ National Socialist, Berlin, 3rd: Tonight, after General Schleicher presented the list of cabinet members, he was formally appointed by the President as Prime Minister and Minister of Defense, as well as Administrative Commissioner of Prussia. He also appointed Dr. Bracht, the former acting Administrative Commissioner of Prussia, as Minister of Interior, Baron von Neurath as Minister of Foreign Affairs, Count Schwerin von Krosigk as Minister of Finance, and Baron von Rüpenach as Minister of Transportation and Post. All three of these departments are held by incumbents. He also appointed Dr. Gürtner as Minister of Justice, Dr. Schlubach, a famous labor insurance scholar, as Minister of Labor, Dr. Gereke as Minister of Unemployment Relief, and Dr. Popitz as Minister without Portfolio and Acting Administrative Commissioner of Prussia. The candidates for Minister of Economy and Minister of Agriculture have not yet been decided. After the new cabinet was formed, all parties turned their attention to what would happen after the Reichstag convened on Tuesday. The Communist Party has officially stated today that it will immediately submit a motion of no confidence in the Schleicher cabinet. The National Socialist Party also issued a formal notice tonight, stating that the Schleicher cabinet cannot meet the needs of the people and cannot be tolerated by the party. However, although these two parties occupy a majority of 295 seats in the 585-seat Reichstag, political circles still hope that a compromise solution can be reached before the opening of the Reichstag to avoid the passage of a vote of no confidence and the re-dissolution of the Reichstag.

▲ National Socialist, Berlin, 3rd: German President Hindenburg sent a letter to outgoing Prime Minister von Papen today, thanking him for his assistance. The wording was very sincere. One section read: "It is only because you firmly and sincerely resigned that I reluctantly granted your request with sorrow. I have always trusted and respected your personality and behavior without diminishing. You have served as Prime Minister and Administrative Commissioner of Prussia for only six months, but your dedication to governance, patriotism, and virtuous character are deeply admired by me. I will never forget the period of our cooperation. I hereby thank you for your achievements in governing the country in the name of the country and myself." Papen also issued a statement today, solemnly stating that the purpose of his past work was only to gather the aspirations of the whole country to see those who value unity and prosperity work together to seek the welfare of the country. Finally, he said, "May we still follow President Hindenburg and work together to create a new Germany."

An employee in the labor unions declared here today that President Hindenburg's appointment of Schleicher to form a cabinet is the best way to resolve the German political crisis.

Situation of the Disarmament Conference 66

British Prime Minister in Busy Talks with Representatives

France Requests New Plan to Be Considered Immediately

Reuters, Geneva, 3rd: British Prime Minister MacDonald was quite busy here today. In the morning, he met with France's Herriot and Paul-Boncour, and in the afternoon, he met with Italian representative Aloisi and American representative Davis. The content of the talks is unknown. It is speculated that this is a preliminary effort to put the Five-Power Conference back on track.

▲ Reuters, Geneva, 3rd: The Japanese naval representative who came here for disarmament matters had a long talk with the British naval representative this afternoon. It is heard that Japan's policy is to submit its proposals after the League of Nations Assembly convenes for other countries' naval discussions. The Italian naval representative met with the American representative this afternoon, but there has been no major progress regarding the French-Italian naval agreement.

▲ Havas, Geneva, 3rd: France has decided to continue the work of the Disarmament Conference by all means, so it has repeatedly requested that the disarmament and security construction plan proposed by France be considered immediately. On Monday, Britain, France and other countries will contact Germany. Yesterday, French Prime Minister Herriot first met with British Prime Minister MacDonald. British Foreign Minister Simon and French Minister of War Paul-Boncour were also present. After the meeting, the general impression was as follows: The interruption of the discussion on disarmament problems is the fault of Germany, and France is not responsible in any way. During the suspension of the discussion, the French delegation prepared a complete plan stipulating a military system that all countries can adopt, and detailed the security conditions that are indispensable for disarmament. The so-called principle of equality of armaments has been given a concrete form after such a plan. The purpose of the Disarmament Conference is to make all countries not restricted by the Treaty of Versailles also disarm uniformly. France does not object to this level, but Germany requests that the principle of equality of armaments be the preamble to the Disarmament Conference. France advocates that security should come first, and the principle of equality of armaments should be the conclusion of the Disarmament Conference. That is, the decision of the Disarmament Conference on July 23 this year also advocated this. The plan proposed by France advocates that the Disarmament Conference should promote a system that allows all countries to enjoy equal security. For this reason, it is not only unfair but also contrary to the purpose of the Disarmament Conference to discuss the armament equality issue separately and urgently seek a solution, and to prevent France from demanding security construction as a price. Germany's revision of its armaments is only subject to the recognition of the countries that signed the Treaty of Versailles. It is estimated that Herriot and Paul-Boncour will not be able to abandon this view during the negotiations in Geneva.

The report declares that when the London Naval Treaty expires in 1936, the U.S. naval strength will be far below the limits stipulated by the treaty. Its destroyers, submarines, light cruisers, and aircraft carriers will be especially far behind Japan. Britain will also greatly reduce its strength in these types of warships. The U.S. Navy's estimated expenditure for the 1933 fiscal year is a total of US$459 million, compared to US$358 million in the previous year.

Persian Government Recovers Oil Rights Dispute 74

Anglo-Persian Oil Company Opposes Cancellation of Concession

Persian Ministry of Finance Replies That It Cannot Rescind the Order

Reuters, Delhi, 3rd: The Anglo-Persian Oil Company has submitted a reply to the Persian Ministry of Finance regarding the Persian government's cancellation of the concession, stating that the company believes the cancellation is unfair and irregular, and therefore does not accept the cancellation. Persia has recognized this concession both before and after the Constitution, so the Persian government has no right to cancel it. The company cannot accept the government's claim that the concession was established before Persia had a Constitution and is now invalid. The company hopes that the Ministry of Finance will withdraw its letter that harms the company's interests. The Ministry of Finance replied that this is the government's final decision and that the department cannot accept the company's proposal.

▲ Havas, Delhi, 3rd: The Persian government has announced the cancellation of the contract between Persia and the Anglo-Persian Oil Company regarding the D'Arcy concession. The Persian Parliament has also passed the cancellation declaration. The Anglo-Persian Oil Company has notified the Persian government that it cannot recognize this cancellation as a legal means. The government replied that the cancellation proposal has been decided and cannot be changed. According to the contract, the Anglo-Persian Oil Company should pay the Persian government 16% of its annual income, but the company suggested to the Persian government to pay about 300,000 pounds as the payment due for 1931 due to the low price of kerosene in the international market. The Persian side deeply believes that the Anglo-Persian Oil Company has not frankly fulfilled the contract. According to the D'Arcy concession, the Anglo-Persian Oil Company obtained it in 1901. Its business began to be well-known in 1905. In 1912, the company paid the Persian government 9,000 pounds. During the European War, although the kerosene mining business did not stop, the company did not pay a penny. It was not until 1920 that it resumed paying. In the following eleven years, the company's profits exceeded 200 million pounds, while the total amount of money received by the Persian government was less than 10 million pounds. Once the above situation was revealed, public opinion was in an uproar. The Persian government intended to set fair terms to protect the interests of the country, so it had to announce the cancellation of the concession contract. For the company, it would be better to correct the above unfair situation in order to eliminate misunderstandings and treat the Persian government with sincerity.

Japanese and Puppet Troops Launch Large-Scale Offensive Against Jilin Volunteer Army 78

National Salvation Army Breaks Through Encirclement on the Jihai Railway

Fu, Zhao, Luo, and Other Units Counterattack After Reinforcements

Tianjin Dispatch: The most vigorous anti-Japanese and traitor-suppression efforts in Jilin Province are being carried out by the Northeast National Salvation Army's 7th Detachment Commander Fu Dianchen, 8th Detachment Commander Zhao Furui (currently represented by Chief of Staff Ma Junshan), and 19th Detachment Commander Luo Mingxing. They attacked Changchun and raided Jilin, shaking the puppet capital. The Jichang and Jihai Railways have been repeatedly destroyed, preventing traffic for a long time. The Japanese and puppet armies fear and hate them deeply. Recently, they launched a large-scale encirclement of Fu, Zhao, Luo, and other units with more than two divisions of troops, Zhang Haipeng's traitorous forces, dozens of aircraft, tanks, artillery, and other new weapons. A fierce battle shook the world. The report on the battle is urgently recorded below:

According to a high-level intelligence report on November 14th at 9:00 AM, Fu Dianchen, commander of the Northeast National Salvation Army's Independent 7th Detachment, learned that Lieutenant General Shaochuan, the puppet commander-in-chief (stationed in Sipingjie), was advancing with four divisions (Japanese soldiers) and 100,000 cavalry from the traitorous army of Zhang Haipeng, attacking the volunteer armies on various railway lines. They attached great importance to the Jichang and Jihai Railways and decided to deploy two divisions of Japanese soldiers and six cavalry brigades of the traitorous army. The advance force, consisting of two cavalry brigades and two Japanese infantry regiments (approximately equivalent to two Chinese mixed regiments), was rushing to the areas occupied by our detachment. After receiving the report, Commander Fu immediately convened a meeting of senior officers. It was generally agreed that after years of hard fighting, our army had been able to win more with less due to guerrilla tactics. However, during this snowy and icy season, the soldiers lacked winter clothing and shoes, and the ammunition reserves were running low and difficult to replenish once used up. Moreover, the Japanese and puppet forces were pressing with heavy troops, and their momentum was fierce. Therefore, it would be better to retreat to preserve strength. It was decided to abandon unimportant areas, shorten the defensive lines, and concentrate forces to break through the Japanese and puppet encirclement and advance to the 囗囗 Mountains to rest and reorganize, waiting for reinforcements before launching a large-scale offensive. Commander Fu immediately ordered the 1st Division Commander Liu Jingchun to lead his troops to cover the retreat (because the division commander was brave and calm in battle, had effective measures, sufficient ammunition, strong soldiers and horses, and the soldiers were mostly local people familiar with the mountain paths). The 1st Division Commander Lin Guiyi led his entire force to serve as the vanguard (the officers and soldiers of this division were mostly Shandong and Lu heroes, brave and good at fighting). The 3rd Division Commander Wang Haishan led his troops to contain the flanks of the Japanese and puppet forces in Shuanghezhen, Pihezi, and other places to facilitate the retreat of our 1st and 2nd Divisions. After the various arrangements were made, Commander Fu led the guard regiment, the entire staff of the headquarters, and important supplies such as provisions, and first retreated from Chaluhe to Badaohe Street to await the assembly of the various divisions. That night, a snowstorm raged, and the exhaled breath turned to ice. The mournful wind howled, causing shivers. The soldiers lacked winter clothing, and the situation was very miserable. However, thinking of the strong enemy ahead, they stood guard with their weapons, their morale soaring a hundredfold, shouting and neighing, awaiting the start of a great battle. On the morning of the 15th, at 2:00 AM, according to reports from various scouts, the Japanese and puppet forces had completed their deployment and were preparing to launch a siege at dawn. The 2nd Division immediately ordered mobilization and launched an attack south of the Jihai Railway. The Japanese and puppet armies fired rifles, machine guns, and artillery simultaneously, the rumbling sound deafening. The fierce artillery fire was beyond description. Our army advanced while maneuvering, fighting as they went. At dawn, they broke through the encirclement, which was completely unexpected by the Japanese and puppet forces, so they continued to pursue and bombard. At around 8:00 AM, our army retreated into the mountains. The 1st Division covered the retreat, setting up defenses on each mountain ridge they occupied. By 9:00 AM, our army had penetrated deep into the mountains. Many of the Japanese and puppet soldiers had become sick from the cold, and they were ambushed by our forces, so they stopped pursuing. Our army was preparing to rest and reorganize the team when Japanese aircraft suddenly arrived, bombing in groups of three. Our army quickly dispersed and took cover. The Japanese planes initially flew low, and we fired rockets at them. Although they did not hit, the Japanese planes were very afraid and dared not fly low. Our army saw that the trees were uprooted and the mountain rocks were shattered where the bombs landed. However, because of avoiding the planes, they stopped advancing. The Japanese and puppet armies attacked again, and the fighting continued until the afternoon of the 16th, when they finally gathered in the planned safe area. In this battle, our officers and soldiers suffered slight casualties, and the ammunition became even more scarce due to two days and one night of fierce fighting. They have now retreated into the 囗囗 Mountains to await supplies and reinforcements.

On the morning of the 14th, at 10:00 AM, the 8th Detachment received intelligence that the Japanese and puppet forces were launching a large-scale encirclement of the 7th Detachment on the Jihai Railway. Chief of Staff Ma Junshan convened a meeting and decided that they could not support the 7th Detachment. They decided to destroy the Jichang Railway and attack the flanks of the Japanese and puppet forces to facilitate the withdrawal of the 7th Detachment. Chief of Staff Ma then directed the 1st Division Commander Wang Hailou and the 2nd Division Commander Zhu Pengji to lead their entire forces to Botuohezi, Duanjiatun, Erdaogou, and other places, together with the 19th Detachment of Luo Mingxing (nicknamed "Three Rivers Hero"), to coordinate their actions. On the night of the 19th, they occupied the Xiajiutai Railway Station (which the puppet government recently planned to rename Jiutai County) and captured the streets, killing more than 400 Japanese and puppet soldiers, seizing more than 700 firearms, capturing more than 1,100 puppet soldiers, and acquiring a large amount of military supplies. At noon on the 20th, the Japanese and puppet forces received reinforcements from nearby and launched a counterattack against our army. Our army withdrew from the streets and occupied positions at the railway station, fighting while simultaneously selecting two special task forces. One team was sent to Yinmahe to destroy bridges, and the other team captured Huapichang Railway Station. The Japanese and puppet forces were attacked from both sides and collapsed on the afternoon of the 21st. Our army returned fully loaded and then went to the border of Shanghegou, Demaxian to concentrate. They are now joining forces with Wang Delin's army at 囗囗 on the Songhua River to await supplies and reinforcements (December 囗 day).

Fang Shengtao and Chen Peikun Have Left Fujian for Shanghai

Internal Reform of the "People's Defense Force" Plan 80

To be Renamed "People's Defense Corps" and Adopt Conscription

A Proposal Has Been Drafted and Submitted to the Internal Affairs Conference for Discussion

The Second National Internal Affairs Conference convened by the Ministry of Interior is scheduled to open in Nanjing on the 10th of this month. The Ministry of Interior believes that this conference will have in-depth discussions on various matters that should be undertaken and reformed, which is greatly related to the future of China's internal affairs. It has drafted a number of important proposals to be submitted to the conference for discussion. It is reported that one of the proposed proposals is to reform the county "Defense Corps," the main purpose of which is to change the current county "Defense Corps" in various provinces into "People's Defense Corps" and adopt a conscription system. The original proposal describes the reasons for the reform and the methods in detail. The methods are recorded as follows: (1) The "Defense Corps" is renamed "People's Defense Corps." (2) The "People's Defense Corps" adopts a conscription system, and hiring substitutes is not allowed. (3) All male citizens of the Republic of China who are between the ages of 20 and 40 are obligated to be incorporated into the "People's Defense Corps" to receive training and serve. (4) The "People's Defense Corps" is divided into four types: active duty corps, reserve corps, first reserve corps, and second reserve corps. (5) The term of active duty is nine months, with the first six months spent in training and the last three months responsible for training the first reserve corps. Upon completion of the term, they are transferred to the reserve corps, which lasts for 囗 years and three months. Upon completion of the term, they are transferred to the second reserve corps. Those who have not been incorporated into the active duty corps are all incorporated into the first reserve corps. Both the first reserve corps and the second reserve corps will continue until they reach the age of service. (6) The active duty corps should be recruited from able-bodied men aged 20 to 24. If the number of people is too large, it will be determined by lot. (7) Those who have one of the following circumstances may be exempted from the obligation to be incorporated into the "People's Defense Corps": (1) those who are disabled or deformed; (2) those who are mentally unsound; (3) those who have no other able-bodied males in the family and whose conscription would make it impossible to maintain their family's livelihood and have reliable proof. (8) Graduates of secondary schools or above who have completed military science courses and have certificates may be directly incorporated into the reserve corps. (9) Those who have one of the following circumstances may postpone their conscription: (1) those who are currently serving in local public office; (2) those who are studying at school; (3) those who are ill or unable to perform labor after illness; (4) those who are being investigated or tried for crimes punishable by penal servitude or more severe; (5) those who have been convicted of crimes and are serving sentences of penal servitude; (6) those who have been released on parole. If the above circumstances have not ended by the time the active duty corps reaches the age of conscription, they will be directly incorporated into the first reserve corps. (10) Although the term of service in the "People's Defense Corps" has expired, it may be extended by order in the event of extraordinary events or special circumstances. (11) The organization of the "People's Defense Corps" is as follows: (1) The province establishes a provincial defense committee under the provincial government to manage the defense affairs of the entire province. The chairman and vice-chairman are concurrently held by the provincial chairman and the director of civil affairs, respectively. (2) The province is divided into several districts, and each district establishes a district defense headquarters to supervise the defense affairs of the district. The district defense commander is appointed by the provincial government upon the recommendation of the provincial defense committee. (3) The county establishes a county defense headquarters to handle the defense affairs of the entire county. The commander is concurrently held by the county magistrate, and the deputy commander is appointed by the provincial defense committee upon the recommendation of the district commander. (12) The district and county defense headquarters shall establish a political training director, a political instructor, and several trainers to be responsible for political training. (13) The county defense headquarters may establish a conscription committee, and each district under the county may establish a branch to be responsible for investigating and compiling the roster of able-bodied men in the county or district, reporting it on a regular basis, and conscripting and convening the "Defense Corps." (14) The active duty corps is organized with ten men as a squad, three squads as a platoon, three platoons as a company, and three or five companies as a battalion. Each county may organize several companies into several battalions depending on the circumstances, and they are led by the county commander and deputy commander. The organization of the reserve corps and the reserve corps is the same as the active duty corps. (15) One-half of the active duty corps retires every half year (four and a half months), and one-half is conscripted to replenish it. (16) The active duty corps is responsible for assisting the military police in pacifying the local area and is generally confined to the county. However, they may carry out their duties in various counties within the defense district upon the order of the district commander. (17) The reserve corps and the reserve corps usually live at home and engage in their occupations, responsible for clearing the countryside. In the event of extraordinary events, they should immediately assemble to respond. (18) In the event of extraordinary events in the country or local area, in addition to dispatching the active duty corps, the reserve corps and the reserve corps may be convened by order. (19) The training of the "People's Defense Corps" is divided into military training and political training, and the subjects are formulated by the provincial defense committee. The "People's Defense Corps" should hold inspections at appropriate times, and the methods are determined by the provincial defense committee. (20) The reserve corps trains for a certain number of days each year. The first reserve corps trains for three months each year for the first three years (12 hours per week). From the fourth year onwards, it is inspected once a year. The second reserve corps is inspected once a year. (21) The flag, clothing, and symbols of the "People's Defense Corps" are formulated by the Ministry of Interior and promulgated. (22) The firearms of the active duty corps are allocated from the existing public guns and corps guns. If they are insufficient, they are purchased and supplemented with local public funds. The firearms of the reserve corps and the reserve corps are requisitioned from all civilian guns during training or wartime, but they are returned to the owners in peacetime. (23) The expenses of the "Defense Corps" in each province are centrally allocated by the provincial government. (24) The budgets of the "Defense Corps" at all levels should be stipulated by the provincial government, and their final accounts should be reported to the provincial government for verification and cancellation on a regular basis. (25) If a member of the active duty corps commits a crime punishable by penal servitude or escapes privately during the term of service, the term of imprisonment or the number of days of escape shall not be counted in the term of service. (26) The "People's Defense Corps" system may be implemented in phases and districts in each province depending on the circumstances.

Songjiang 81

Telegraph Request to the Provincial Government

To Exempt from Levying Borrowed Grain

The provincial government instructed this county to continue to levy two yuan of "borrowed grain" when collecting the second installment of land tax to offset the needs of suppressing bandits and providing sufficient funds. Now, the various industries in this county are experiencing a decline in rice prices, and rents have decreased by one-third compared to last year, causing extreme economic hardship for the people. Therefore, Li Zuhua, Cai Zhongyu, and Wu Qianmei, the director and deputy directors of the Public Funds and Property Management Office, telegraphed to the Director of Finance of the Provincial Government and Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance, stating: "We have investigated that last year, an additional two yuan of grain silver was levied for each stone of grain, and the people appealed to be exempted from the levy because the burden was too heavy. We were fortunate to receive your order that the additional two yuan of grain for this year's commutation of grain tax was for military expenses to suppress bandits and could not be offset. We presented a request for approval to extend the additional levy for one year. We admire your concern for the people's livelihood and your provisional measures, which have been restricted. The people are also mindful of the provincial treasury's deficit, so they have to reluctantly contribute to fulfill their obligations, as the additional grain levy is not long-lasting. However, although last year's harvest was not abundant, the rice price was not low, so they could still bear the pain and pay. This year, the rice price has fallen sharply, and the farmers' rental income is less than two-thirds of last year's. The people's suffering is even greater than before, and the second installment of land tax is being levied, with an additional two yuan of grain being levied continuously. Our officials have been entrusted by the local elders and dare not remain silent. We telegraph to request exemption from the additional levy of two yuan of 'borrowed grain' per stone this year to alleviate the people's hardship."

Tinglin Feng Family

Robbed Twice

The family of Feng Bingjun, a resident of Fenghuotang Township in Tinglin, used to be well-off but was robbed once before, suffering heavy losses. However, Feng Bingjun worked hard and lived frugally. After the robbery, he tightened his belt even more. In recent years, he gradually recovered his former state. Unexpectedly, a group of bandits armed with box cannons broke into his house again the other night, forcing the victim to reveal the location of his hidden silver. The bandits looted the inner rooms and escaped with more than 1,000 silver dollars. The victim has reported the case to the police station to track down the stolen goods and the bandits.

Suzhou 82

Kidnappers Carrying Victim

Arrested on a Train

Yesterday morning (the 4th), at around 2:00 AM, three bandits armed with handguns suddenly arrived at the home of Li Jinqing, a resident of Tianpingshan in Mudu, and looted at will. Before leaving, they kidnapped Li Yuchang (age 14). By 6:00 AM, the bandits and their victim were at Suzhou Railway Station, planning to take a train to Shanghai to demand a ransom. Unexpectedly, the victim reported to the railway police at the station, who arrested one bandit named Lin Chunfa from Jiaxing. It is said that two other bandits escaped when they heard the alarm.

Got Up to Light a Lamp

Suddenly Collapsed and Died

Zhongli (31 years old, from Baoying), the brother of Liu Zhongying, the owner of Yiji Hat Workshop at No. 87 Jiqing Street inside Xumen, said he felt uncomfortable at around 1:00 AM yesterday morning (the 4th). He got up, fumbled for a match to light a lamp, and suddenly collapsed. His brother heard the noise and rushed over to see that he was already stiff and cold to the touch. By 2:00 PM, he had purchased clothes and a coffin and was preparing to put the body in the coffin when he suddenly saw blood coming from the deceased's nose, his heart was beating, his limbs were warm, and he was moving. Initially suspecting a zombie, they realized that he had indeed come back to life. They called Dr. Nie Jimin of Dongwu Hospital for a consultation, but he died of exhaustion by 4:00 PM in the evening.

Wuxi 83

Organizing Deteriorated Silk

Application for Extension

Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the Wuxi Silk Factory Guild held its 20th temporary membership meeting at the Xujia Alley Guild Hall. Representatives from 17 factories, including Yongtai, and 15 people, including Xue Shouhuan, attended. Qian Fengting, the chairman, discussed the following matters: (1) Reporting the letter from the Jiangzhe Deteriorated Silk and Cocoons Organization Committee instructing the factories that have registered their deteriorated silk and cocoons to affix the registration seal to the original notification letter issued by the organization committee and submit it to the guild for compilation and remittance to serve as proof for issuing registration forms to clarify the number of households that have already received forms. It has been found that the deadline for subsidizing deteriorated silk and cocoons at the end of December is approaching rapidly, and only 9,540 bales of silk have been exported to date. More than 17,000 loads of silk that have been registered and stamped have not been exported. The Organizing Committee is currently trying to request an extension, but the procedures are very complicated, and it is still unknown whether the government will approve it. All factories are requested to submit the registration forms as soon as possible and not delay any longer. As for the subsidies, it was originally planned to issue treasury bonds, but now it has been changed to public debt. If you have any opinions, please express them. It was resolved that factories that have not yet filled out the registration forms should submit them to the guild as soon as possible for compilation and remittance, and that the deteriorated silk that has already been produced must be exported by the deadline.

Provincial Defense Committee

Comes to Wuxi for Inspection

Yuan Xiluo of the Jiangsu Provincial Defense Committee recently set out from Zhenjiang to inspect the defense corps of the four counties of Wuxi, Jiangyin, Yixing, and Jinshan in preparation for implementing political training for the defense corps in all counties of the province. Currently, the two counties of Qidong and Chongming are doing the best in Jiangsu Province's defense corps. Therefore, it is planned to send personnel to visit and investigate the above two places in the short term. I am currently planning to go to Jiangyin for inspection first, stay for about two or three days, and then come to Wuxi for inspection, he said.

Hangzhou 85

Zhexi Seawall

Construction Completed

The seawall project along the Qiantang River estuary in Western Zhejiang is a massive undertaking with a long history, a great architectural feat of the old era. Due to years of disrepair, in the autumns of the 19th and 20th years of the Republic, continuous wind and rain and sudden tides threatened the embankments of the 8th, 9th, 10th, and 11th forts of Hai'ning County. The Construction Department ordered the Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau to carry out emergency repairs. Afterwards, the dangerous sections of each fort were selected and rebuilt using new seawall construction methods. However, the cost was quite high, and the dangerous seawalls of Western Zhejiang are not only related to the three old prefectures of Hangzhou, Jiaxing, and Huzhou in Western Zhejiang, but also the lives and properties of the people of the Suzhou, Songjiang, Changzhou, and Taicang prefectures of Jiangsu Province depend entirely on this seawall for protection. Therefore, a request was submitted to the National Government to allocate funds for major repairs. After approval by the Executive Yuan, 2 million yuan in disaster relief bonds were allocated, but these bonds could not be mortgaged because they had not been issued. The Zhejiang Provincial Government could not delay the demolition and construction of the seawall, so it raised funds separately and selected important sections for construction. Since the start of construction, the most dangerous sections of the Ming, Pan, Yi, Mi, Yu, Ji, Po, Mu, Qin, Bing, Yue, Zong, and other characters have been demolished and completed, requiring a total of 250,000 yuan in construction funds. Yesterday (the 3rd), a completion ceremony was held at the temporary construction site of the dangerous seawall section of the Hanghai section of the Pan Ming character. The Construction Department invited representatives from all walks of life to visit in advance. Zeng Yangfu, the Director of the Construction Department, Zhang Zili, the Director of the Water Conservancy Bureau, Du Zhenhuan, the Director of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Bureau, Xiao Aishi, a foreign expert of the Provincial Government, Fang Qingru, the representative of the Provincial Party Department, and 40 other people departed from Hangzhou by car at 8:00 AM, inspected from the 11th Fort to Wangba Fort along the way, and took a group photo before holding the completion ceremony. It is reported that the demolition and construction of the most dangerous seawalls was carried out with great frugality, costing a total of 250,000 yuan. If all the seawalls are completely repaired, it will cost an estimated 1.6 million yuan. If the original plan can be fully implemented, the lives and properties of the people of the three prefectures of Hangzhou, Jiaxing, and Huzhou in Western Zhejiang and the prefectures of Suzhou, Songjiang, Changzhou, and Taicang in Jiangsu Province will be fully guaranteed in the future. (the 3rd)

Anqing 86

Grain and Wheat Surtax

Cease Collection

Anhui Province issued hundreds of thousands of road construction bonds due to the importance of road construction and designated the grain surtax as the road construction bond fund. However, the natives of the capital, Shanghai, and Anhui strongly opposed it. The provincial government, fearing that it would affect the road debt, strongly advocated caution. On the 2nd, at the 308th regular meeting of the provincial government, Chairman Wu Zhongxin proposed a proposal to exempt all grain export surtaxes, stating that the grain export surtax case in this province has been designated as a special fund for road construction, but recently the rice price has plummeted, and the rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy. In order to provide relief, it is proposed to exempt all grain export surtaxes in this province, and the road construction funds will be submitted to the central government for separate arrangements. It was resolved that all grain surtaxes in the province should be stopped.

Support Association Remits Funds to Encourage Volunteer Army 87

Fierce Battle Begins in Northern Manchuria

Survival of the Northeast at Stake

Telegraph Request to Incite a Pincer Attack

The Shanghai Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association believes that the Japanese 5th Division is launching a large-scale attack to oppress the volunteer army and that a fierce battle has already begun. Yesterday, they telegraphed Li Du, Ding Chao, Wang Delin, and others separately and remitted funds to provide assistance, requesting that they encourage the entire army to bravely kill the enemy. The original telegram is as follows:

Since Commander Su Hanzhang swore an oath to resist Japan in Northern Manchuria, the situation has changed, international sympathy has been gained, and the stubborn enemy has become angry and is now driving five divisions of Japanese troops to oppress us on a large scale. A fierce battle has already begun. Although the Su and Ma armies have natural barriers to rely on, they have no confidence in winning. We request that the volunteer armies of Jilin Province incite and launch a pincer attack in various directions. The opportunity is difficult to repeat. All China National Salvation United Association

Invites Liu Piguang to Report

Conditions of Resistance Against Japan in Jilin and Heilongjiang 88

The China Eastern News Agency reports that the Joint Federation of National Salvation Organizations from all sectors of the country invited Mr. Liu Piguang, the representative of Ding Chao and Li Du from the Joint Communication Office in Shanghai of the Northeastern Anti-Japanese Armies, to report on the recent combat situation of the Northeastern Volunteer Army at the federation's meeting yesterday (the 4th) afternoon. The attendees included council members of the federation Zhang Jun'guang, Tu Liang, Dong Mosheng, Zuo Hua, Xie Nai'shi, Chen Zhenquan, Ma Zhiying, etc. The meeting commenced at 2:30 PM. After Chairman Zhang Jun'guang delivered a speech, Mr. Liu began his report, saying: "I am very grateful for the invitation to report to you today. I originally planned to discuss things in detail, but I have been ill these past few days, so I can only give a simple and unordered report on the recent situation in Jilin and Heilongjiang. I apologize deeply."

▲ Regarding Heilongjiang Province

You all know very well the past situation of anti-Japanese warfare in Heilongjiang Province. I will only talk about the recent situation. Recently, the northwestern part of Heilongjiang is completely occupied by Su Bingwen's troops, and the northeastern part is occupied by Ma Zhanshan's troops. Su Bingwen's revolt was carefully planned and prepared in advance, so his strength has been very powerful since the uprising. Therefore, the Japanese have also concentrated all their forces to suppress Su's army. However, Su's army has not succumbed. Since merging with Ma Zhanshan's troops, their resistance has become even greater. The total strength of Su and Ma is now about 100,000, with 50,000 to 60,000 concentrated in the Greater Khingan Range. The west of the Greater Khingan Range is completely under Su's influence, and the southeast is under Ma's influence. The Japanese forces are only in the Qiqihar, Hailun, and Harbin areas, along the railway line. Recently, because the Heilongjiang army is concentrated in the Greater Khingan Range, the Japanese army has also concentrated there, so the decisive battle in the future will be in the Greater Khingan Range, and the victory or defeat will also be in the Greater Khingan Range.

▲ Regarding Jilin Province

In Jilin Province, the area around the Mudan River and east of the Songhua River, west of the Russian Primorsky Krai, is completely under the influence of Ding and Li. There have been no major battles there recently. Only more than ten days ago, the Yilan line in the lower reaches of the Songhua River was completely recaptured by Li Du, so the lost territory along the Songhua River has been restored. The current battle plan is to disrupt the Japanese rear from Yilan to Harbin. The Japanese have already become fearful of this, so they have also concentrated heavy troops in Harbin. As for Wang Delin, he is fully cooperating with Ding and Li. After Wang Delin's troops destroyed the construction of the Jihui Line, it can be said to be a great strategic success, making it impossible for the Japanese to complete their military communication line. Wang's current strength is about 50,000, and Ding and Li's strength is about 80,000.

▲ Recent Situation of the Volunteer Army in Jilin and Heilongjiang

About twenty counties in Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces have not been taken away. The postal service of the Republic of China still operates normally there, and the Blue Sky White Sun flag is flying everywhere. It is truly heartbreaking that only this small piece of clean land remains in thousands of miles of beautiful rivers and mountains. The Jilin and Heilongjiang armies are currently experiencing extreme difficulties in terms of supplies and military needs. Last year was relatively manageable, but this year it is simply unimaginable because the army has grown in the past year, so the needs have naturally increased. There were no unlined or single-layered garments this spring and summer, so the soldiers had to remove the cotton wadding from their cotton clothes. Now that winter has arrived, and there is no more cotton wadding to wrap around their bodies. Although some units have requisitioned quilts from the people to make cotton clothes, the number of quilts is limited, which is not enough to keep the soldiers warm. Therefore, most soldiers are still wearing single-layered or unlined clothes and fighting the enemy in the frozen wilderness. Most of the food is taken from the people. Unfortunately, there was a flood in the Songhua River area this year, and the autumn harvest is hopeless, so there is also great concern about food. As for the lack of guns and ammunition, it is even more obvious.

▲ Tactics of the Volunteer Army

The Japanese army completely uses battle lines to suppress the Volunteer Army, but this is not important. The Volunteer Army can use guerrilla tactics to deal with them, making it impossible for them to cope. Moreover, the Volunteer Army's shooting is very accurate, and one bullet can always take down an enemy. However, the Japanese army's artillery, airplanes, and bombs are something that the Volunteer Army cannot deal with, because the Volunteer Army does not have such sophisticated weapons. Therefore, the Japanese can only use artillery and bombs to bombard the Volunteer Army during the day. The Volunteer Army can only attack at night. At present, the Japanese forces rely entirely on important cities along the South Manchurian, Beining, Tao'ang, and Chinese Eastern Railways. Otherwise, there are no traces of them. As for the Volunteer Army, they appear and disappear everywhere, using guerrilla tactics to make it difficult for the Japanese army to cope. Although the Volunteer Army has the strength to recapture important cities, it is difficult to defend them after recapture due to the lack of guns and ammunition. In order to avoid major losses, it is better not to recapture them for the time being. If the national government can provide effective assistance, then it will not be difficult to recover the Eastern Provinces.

▲ Failure of Japanese Aggression

The Japanese imperialists' occupation of our Eastern Provinces was originally intended to alleviate their own crisis through economic aggression in the Three Northeastern Provinces. However, since the occupation of the Three Northeastern Provinces by the Japanese for a year and the establishment of a puppet government, the resistance and disruption of the Volunteer Army have caused complete chaos in the Three Northeastern Provinces. Commerce is depressed, and the economy is bankrupt. The Japanese economic aggression in the Northeast cannot be successfully completed. Therefore, it goes without saying that the Volunteer Army can persist in fighting the Japanese, and the economic aggression of Japanese imperialism has failed. At the same time, Japan's immigration policy has also completely failed. Although they have worked hard to carry out their so-called armed immigration since September 18, these immigrants are constantly subjected to the oppression of the Volunteer Army. Now, the past immigrants have all fled or committed suicide due to economic bankruptcy, and it is of course even more difficult for new immigrants to gain a foothold. Therefore, since September 18, Japan's immigration policy has also completely failed.

▲ Atrocities of the Japanese Army in the Northeast

The Japanese army arbitrarily kills our people. After September 18 last year, the frontline soldiers who returned from the battle at the Nenjiang Bridge all saw with their own eyes the Japanese capturing Chinese people one by one, hanging them upside down on the bridge, and slowly stabbing them to death with knives. As for Chinese people being buried alive in various places, it is even more commonplace. The method of burying alive is to have the person being buried dig a mud cave himself, crawl into the cave himself, and cover it with mud himself. Finally, the Japanese completely bury the person with mud. Sometimes they also arbitrarily arrest a Chinese person, accuse him of being suspicious, and beat him severely with leather whips, even pouring kerosene and chili water into his nostrils and mouth. In important cities, there is a health inspection or household survey every few days. During the survey, the Japanese arbitrarily break into people's homes, arbitrarily beat men, and rape women. Especially those female students are insulted beyond description. The suffering of our people under the iron heel of Japanese imperialism is no different from that of slaves of a conquered nation.

▲ Efforts That the Chinese People Should Make

The loss of the Three Northeastern Provinces is originally a very painful matter. Although the Volunteer Army's fighting against Japan is not strong, the blow it has given to Japan is already very deep. It can be seen that the only way to avenge the national humiliation is through force. However, the strength of the Volunteer Army is very weak, and it is difficult to win without the assistance of the people of the whole country. Therefore, in this time of national crisis, all Chinese people should do their best to help the Volunteer Army, both spiritually and materially. Only through such continuous efforts can we put the enemy to death, wash away the national shame, and recover the lost territory. As for donations and assistance from all sectors, it is best to remit them directly to that side, not only is telegraphic transfer still available there, but it also avoids many troubles. This is also something that I am specifically mentioning to you today in my report. Although there is a lot more to say, I have to end here due to time constraints and my illness. After Mr. Liu finished his report, everyone dispersed after receiving refreshments.

He Yingqin's Remarks 90

Hubei Bandits and Jiangxi Bandits Can Be Expected to Be Suppressed

Guizhou War and Sichuan War to Be Handled Separately

Minister of Military Administration He Yingqin came to Shanghai the day before yesterday for medical treatment due to illness. A reporter from the Central News Agency visited Mr. He at his residence yesterday to inquire about the situation of bandit suppression and matters in Guizhou and Sichuan. Mr. He graciously received him and answered in detail. The following is a separate record:

Situation of Bandit Suppression

According to Minister He, the bandits in Hubei have been largely dispersed after being severely suppressed by the National Army. At present, only a few small groups remain, such as the Xu bandits who are fleeing westward towards the Shaanxi border. Yang Hucheng has sent troops to intercept them, and they will soon be completely suppressed. There are currently still 20,000 communist bandits in Jiangxi. Recently, they attempted to flee to eastern Jiangxi, planning to first occupy Fuzhou and then attack Xuguigui, Yiyang, and other places. The National Army has detected this and is intercepting them fiercely. They have now fled towards the border of Jiangxi and Fujian, to Lichuan, Jianning, and Taining. The National Army has also advanced from Fuzhou to Huwan to pursue them. The military affairs of bandit suppression in Jiangxi Province are being directed by me remotely from Beijing. Recently, General Chen Cheng has been appointed as the commander of the forward troops advancing on Fuzhou. Commander Chiang will go to Jiangxi to supervise the suppression of bandits as soon as the Third Plenary Session is over. It is expected that they will be completely suppressed in the near future.

Internal Strife in Guizhou and Sichuan 91

Regarding Guizhou, I previously received a telegram from You Guocai stating that You's troops have already occupied Guiyang, and Wang Jialie's troops have retreated towards western Guizhou. However, I have not yet received a report from Wang Jialie. According to another source, He Zizhong's division of Wang Jialie's troops was originally stationed on the border of Guizhou and Hunan. Wang has now telegraphed He's division to rush to aid. You Guocai intends to intercept He's division midway to eliminate Wang's strength. As for the truth, it is still unclear. The Central Government must wait until the truth is ascertained before making a decision on how to deal with it. It has already been decided to reorganize the Sichuan government based on the order of the 17th year of the Republic of China. However, the Central Government has not yet decided whether to establish a reorganization committee.

Third Plenary Session 92

The Third Plenary Session is a regular meeting held once a year. This session is scheduled to open in Beijing on the 15th. I will of course attend, but there are no proposals circulating. I have not heard of the rumors that this meeting will discuss raising the chairman's authority and increasing the number of standing committee members of the Central Political Council.

Returning to Beijing Today 93

I came to Shanghai this time for medical treatment and have no other tasks. Last Friday, I suddenly had a fever all over my body and discovered red rashes that were extremely itchy. Therefore, I came to Shanghai for medical treatment late at night. I have now recovered slightly and plan to return to Beijing tomorrow (i.e., today) by night train.

Li Jingcong Discusses the Importance of Opening the Northwest Air Route 95

▲ Can Shorten the Schedule of Mail to Europe

A reporter from the Nihon Shinbun visited Li Jingcong, the Director of the General Affairs Department of the Ministry of Communications, at his private residence yesterday to inquire about the details of the Eurasia Company's Northwest Air Administration. Mr. Li said: Since the September 18th Incident, the government has implemented a blockade of postal services in the Northeast. All mail to Europe has been ordered to be transported via the Suez Canal, which takes at least a month to arrive. In order to save time, Chinese and foreign people often cannot sympathize with the government's difficulties and privately submit their mail to a certain party in the hope that it can still be transported via Siberia. However, even with this kind of submission, it still takes at least 20 days or more to arrive. After the opening of the Northwest Air Route, if all mail to Europe can be transported by plane to Tacheng on the Sino-Russian border (from Shanghai to Tacheng, it takes about three days in winter), and then transferred by train to Xihuo (from Tacheng to Xihuo Bolu, it takes about four days), in order to be transferred by train to Europe (from Xihuo Bolu to Europe, it takes about seven or eight days), then it can be delivered in at most 14 or 15 days. If, in the future, the company's planes can carry mail directly to Europe via Russia, or Russian planes can fly to Tacheng in order to connect with Eurasian planes, then it can be delivered in at most six or seven days. Minister Zhu (Jiahua) believes that whether the Northwest Air Route can only fly to Tacheng, or can fly directly to Europe, or can connect at the Sino-Russian border, it is faster to transport by this method than by any other method, and it is enough to restore vested interests so that there is no more malfeasance of privately submitting mail to a certain party for transfer and to achieve the purpose of implementing a blockade of postal services in the Northeast. Therefore, he attaches great importance to this air route and has repeatedly instructed me to urge Mr. Schmidt, the director of the Aviation Group of the Eurasia Aviation Company, to complete the trial flight work. The No. 5 aircraft that successfully trialed the Northwest has already returned to Shanghai with me the day before yesterday and is actively preparing to proceed in order to open the route when the Third Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee convenes on the 15th of this month. As for the rumors that I will be appointed as the general manager of the company, they are not true. Since I have been the Director of the General Affairs Department of the Ministry of Communications, I have been so busy with affairs that I can hardly leave Beijing. I have no energy to take on such an important position. Because the Ministry's affairs are urgently waiting to be dealt with, I have decided to return to Beijing by overnight train tomorrow night (i.e., tonight).

Female Aviator Lin Pengxia Goes to Xinjiang Alone 96

▲ Has Now Passed Tongguan and is Advancing Towards Xi'an

The Nihon Shinbun reports that Ms. Lin Pengxia, a female aviator from our country, has reached Tongguan at the end of the month after leaving Shanghai on the 24th and is now advancing towards Xi'an. Ms. Lin sent a letter yesterday to her friend Mr. Xu Tongxun in Shanghai, reporting on the life of the people in the Northwest, saying that the people all live in simple earthen pits and the conditions are extremely difficult. However, the road is still relatively peaceful, which is more peaceful than the banditry that is prevalent in the South. The ultimate goal of this trip is to go to Xinjiang, Tibet, Qinghai, and other places to conduct inspections and make detailed development plans for future reference, she said.

Land Acquisition Case by the Ministry of Railways 97

▲ Yu Youren Inspects in Disguise

▲ Villagers Demand Thorough Investigation

Let's See the Spirit of the President of the Control Yuan

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the Ministry of Railways' requisition of land from the residents of Pengpu Zhenru and other districts to build a new station has not been properly resolved due to the villagers' fierce opposition. It is now heard that in addition to appealing to all sectors for sympathy, the villagers also suspect that there may be other reasons for the Ministry of Railways to requisition so much land when so little is needed. They have submitted a petition to the Control Yuan requesting an investigation. Yu Youren, the President of the Control Yuan, believing that the matter is of great importance, made an unofficial inspection yesterday in disguise, taking his wife and daughters in a car to Pengpu. He was seen by the villagers, who immediately sent representatives to request the Control Yuan to send personnel to thoroughly investigate the inside story of the Ministry of Railways' land acquisition. Mr. Yu immediately replied that the content of this matter is not simple and that he is not in a position to express anything as a government official. However, he can conduct a detailed investigation after returning to Beijing and then handle it impartially, he said. Mr. Yu then inspected for a week and left, returning to his residence, it is said.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Receives a Letter from the Customs: Machine-Made Factory Goods Are Not Allowed to Be Exempt from Tax 98

The Jianghai Customs replied to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday, saying: In reply to your letter No. 275, the Shanghai Chinese Candle Industry Association forwarded a report from its member Henry Factory stating that candles shipped to and from the wharf to the inland are being ordered to be detained by the Nanshi office of the Jianghai Customs, claiming that Henry Factory is registered with the Customs and must pay taxes, while Huali Factory is not registered and can be loaded, etc. It is found that goods from Henry and Huali machine-made factories have been handled in accordance with domestic goods tax rates since the Jinjing Tax Office was abolished. Now, those who are registered pay taxes, while those who are not registered are exempt from taxes. Please consult the Tax Affairs Department to handle the matter fairly in accordance with the regulations, etc. It is now learned that the Tax Affairs Department has replied that national goods transported by civil ships from one coastal port to another or to the inland are no longer taxed, except for the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Suzhou route. However, the treatment of goods from machine-made factories is still handled in the same way. This Customs has not received any clear orders and is not in a position to change the established case. It is hereby replied accordingly, I hope you will check accordingly, etc.

Recent News on the Construction of the Songhu Memorial Village 99

▲ Soon to Be Completed One After Another The Songhu Memorial Village is being built with donations from Shanghai citizens, local maintenance associations, and overseas Chinese in Singapore, Mufu, and Basheng. When the Songhu Memorial Village Committee was established, it was during the summer season. Committee members Hu Yunqiu, Kui Yanfang, etc., together with people from various war zones, Wang Binyan, Zhang Xiaoliang, Zhu Kaichou, Yang Weiyu, Jin Jushan, and architect Jin Tongyin, etc., braved the hot weather to run around the fields and plan the construction. Those that have been completed successively are in Taicang County, including 30 village houses in Taoyuan Township, 40 village houses in Nan Village, Yiqiao, 35 village houses in North Village, Yiqiao, 5 assembly halls, 37 village houses in Xintang Village, 3 assembly halls, 37 village houses in South Kou, Qile, 5 assembly halls, 27 village houses in North Kou, Qile, and 2 assembly halls. In Jiading County, there are 56 village houses in North Gate Outside Village, 5 assembly halls, 97 village houses in Maqiao Village, 5 assembly halls, and 5 schoolhouses. In Baoshan County, there are 71 village houses in Miaohang Village, 5 assembly halls, 11 schoolhouses, 50 village houses in Zhuyuan Dun Village, 110 village houses in Sanbai Mu Village, 68 village houses in Shiziqiao Village, 44 village houses in Lvqitang Village, 40 village houses in Guijiaqiao Village, and 264 village houses in Dachang Street. Those that have been built but not yet completed are 132 village houses in Gaojing Temple Village, Jiangwan, with one assembly hall and one schoolhouse each, 217 village houses in Wusong Village, 190 village houses in Zhabei Village, 29 village houses in Pengpu Village, 26 village houses in Zhenru Village, and 34 village houses in Yinhang Village in various districts of Shanghai. In Jiading County, there are 46 Lou Tang Street houses. In addition, there are Jiangwan, Wusong, and other unbuilt village houses that are being re-examined and can also be built soon. At that time, due to the large disaster area and limited funds, although the funds were allocated as appropriate, they were still insufficient. Moreover, the disaster victims had no home to return to and were exposed to the wind and dew, which was extremely pitiful. In order to achieve universality and emergency response, the materials and structures were as economical and simple as possible, without taking beauty into account. The cost of each room was only around 150 yuan. It is now heard that the Shanghai War Zone Relief Committee has allocated funds for relief to the disaster victims in the war zone, and a part of it is also used for building houses, which is being carried out in an orderly manner and will be gradually completed, which can be regarded as coming to an end. However, in order to prevent miscellaneous use of old bricks during the construction of the village houses, the walls have not been plastered. Now, in the places where the construction has been completed, we are taking advantage of the time before it freezes to rush to use paper muscle to plaster the walls to make them stronger.

Ministry of Communications Rectifies Shanghai Telephone Service 100

▲ Connection Fee to Be Abolished

In order to rectify the Shanghai telephone service, in addition to ordering the bureau to quickly repair the damaged landlines in Zhabei and other places during the Shanghai war so that the installed automatic machines can be called on schedule, the Ministry of Communications also believes that the connection fee of five cents for each call between the Chinese area and the concession is neither economical for users nor convenient. After the landline materials in the Chinese and concession areas are laid, the originally scheduled connection fee will be abolished and other methods will be formulated. The Shanghai bureau has been ordered to prepare a detailed plan for submission and approval.
