Enthusiastic Donations to the Righteous Army 102

The following donations from various parties were received yesterday by the Righteous Army Relief Association from various locations: "Zhenjiang Fire Brigade" - A letter from the Zhenjiang First Fire Brigade stated that the Wenhua Bank in their area had specially gifted 100 yuan to the brigade's members as a reward for their participation in the fire fighting at the Pilian Fengxiang Silver Shop, which fortunately prevented the fire from spreading. The brigade felt that firefighting was a public service and should not accept financial rewards to avoid creating a competitive atmosphere on the fire ground and losing the true meaning of public welfare. They unanimously decided to send the full amount to your association to be forwarded to the front lines as a small contribution. This is remitted through the Shanghai Bank. Please accept it - Wu Ji-Yu.

Yu Yan-Zi from the Guanghua Printing Bureau in Yancheng, Wu Ji-Yu, sent a letter stating that on the occasion of his fourth son Yin-Sheng's joyful event, he would contribute 100 yuan saved from the celebration expenses. The money was remitted through the Yancheng Farmers Bank to the Shanghai Xinhua Bank for transfer. "New Fujian Daily" - Chen Chiping, the director of the New Fujian Daily, first collected 1,170 yuan and 55 cents. "Cheng Zhi National Salvation Association" - 18 yuan from the Cheng Zheng National Salvation Association at 54, South Hang Street, Fuzhou.

▲ Xiangcheng Silk Factory Donates to the Righteous Army: The entire workforce of the Xiangcheng Silk Factory on Tiantong Road, Hongkou, adhering to the principle that everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the nation, donated money to support the volunteer army so that they can sustain the fight against Japan. Five donation methods were formulated and unanimously adopted: 1. All colleagues will donate 10% of their November salary. 2. Those who engage in game-like activities such as gambling during their spare time will donate 20 cents each. 3. Those who purchase new clothes that are not domestic products will donate according to the purchase price. 4. Those who consume luxury items will donate 30% of the price of the item. A large bamboo tube will be placed for people to donate at any time. It will be inspected once a month, and if it is full of 10 yuan, it will be sent to the Relief Association. The 88 yuan and 70 cents donated from 10% of the November salary will be sent to the Relief Association for verification.

▲ Chaozhou Fellow Townsmen Association Fund-raising Method: The Northeast Volunteer Army is sacrificing for the country while fighting outside Shanhaiguan and is in urgent need of assistance. Those who cannot take up arms should provide financial assistance. The Chaozhou Fellow Townsmen Association has specially proposed six donation methods. Donations are divided into four types. The donation methods are listed below: 1. Sales Donation: The store determines the number of days and allocates a certain percentage of the daily sales as a donation. 2. Employee Monthly Donation: With six months as the temporary period, all employees will contribute a certain percentage of their salary as a monthly donation. 3. Family Monthly Donation: The head of the family donates a certain amount every day, and the children and servants donate a certain amount each per day (such as a certain number of copper coins to arouse the family's patriotic awareness). 4. Individual Donation: Those who cannot donate in accordance with the above three items are welcome to donate freely, either once or monthly. 5. Public Fundraising: The Association will issue several donation booklets. Please ask the Association's directors and enthusiastic patriotic fellow villagers to carry the booklets to solicit donations. The type of donation should be filled in the booklet. For family and individual donations, the amount should also be filled in. 6. Remitting Donations: At the end of each month, the donations will be sent to the Association for collection in order to gather funds or purchase goods, or the cash will be properly transferred at any time. The names of the donors and the amount of money will be posted in the Association and published in the Association's monthly magazine.

▲ Yousheng Troupe Performs Drama to Raise Funds: In view of the suffering of the compatriots in the Northeast and the arduous battles of the volunteer army, the Yousheng Traveling Troupe performed a drama yesterday at the Tianchan Stage to provide assistance. The order was maintained by the 270, 299, and the Tongyi Public School Children's Army. By 2 PM, the theater was packed with 3,000 people. The performance began with a performance by the Troupe's national music group, followed by speeches by Mr. Tan Bozhi and lawyer Wu Mielu, who briefly described the suffering of the people in the Northeast and our duty to the Northeast. Then, the chairman reported on everything, followed by a performance by the China Harmonica Association. At 2:30 PM, Peking Opera was performed. Mr. Hu Yimeng and Mr. Rong Boming performed "Meilong Town". Mr. Guo and Mr. Wang Zhenming performed the full version of "Lu Yao Knows Horsepower". Mr. Wang Jinkui, Mr. Chen Niuzhong, and Mr. Liu Junlin performed "Heroic Righteousness" as the finale. Mr. Zhu Lianfu, Mr. Rong Boming, Mr. Wu Laopu, Mr. Wu Jiangfeng, and Mr. Wang Zhenming performed the full version of "Four Jinshi". All the gentlemen are senior figures in the amateur opera circles and are very experienced. The performance was very exciting. It is reported that all expenses were borne by the Troupe, and the ticket revenue of approximately 3,000 yuan will be used for Northeast donations.

▲ Leshan Society Generously Donates Public Gifts: The 27th was the auspicious day for the wedding of Mr. Chen Liangyu's grandson. The Leshan Society's entire staff congratulated him with a performance at the Honglou in the French Concession. Mr. Chen was initially unwilling to accept the gifts, but since the Society members were enthusiastic about relief efforts and bore the expenses themselves, he agreed to transfer all the public gifts received from relatives and friends to the Northeast and Henan, Hubei, and Anhui disaster relief funds for the benefit of relatives and friends. On that day, the guests filled the hall, and a total of 443 yuan in public gifts were received and fully transferred to relief efforts. "A cup of water may not be much, but it is still a small help." Such kindness and generosity are commendable.

Inspection Record of the Completion of the Dike Project by the National Flood Relief Association (7) 104

The Anhui Provincial Government Tea Party Inspection Team returned to the ship at 5:30 PM, and the Jiangxin ship set sail at 6:00 PM and arrived in Anqing at 7:30 PM. Wu Zhongxin, Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, and the heads of various departments personally boarded the ship to welcome the team. Military police were densely stationed at the pier, and military music was played in unison. All the team members then disembarked and walked to the nearby Reception Hall outside the South Gate to attend the tea party hosted by the Anhui Provincial Government. During the party, Chairman Wu Zhongxin delivered a welcome speech, stating that he represented the people of Anhui Province in extending a warm welcome to the guests for their inspection visit. He expressed special gratitude to the National Flood Relief Association for building more than a thousand miles of dikes in Anhui Province, which benefited the disaster victims and enabled the rapid recovery of the rural economy.

Politics and Economy: Wu stated that he would like to present the Anhui Provincial Government's recent measures to the guests. Regarding the construction part, he requested Director Liu Yiyan of the Construction Department to report. He stated that in terms of politics and economy, the provincial government had recently made every effort to maintain social order, so it attached great importance to bandit suppression. Fortunately, the banditry in western Anhui had been quelled in recent months, and even small groups of bandits had been completely eliminated. He was now actively handling the aftermath and organizing rehabilitation matters. The finances of Anhui Province had been reduced from more than 16 million yuan to more than 8 million yuan, and the income and expenditure were just enough to offset each other. In addition, there was a special budget of approximately 4 million yuan for construction projects. If this could be maintained, he firmly believed that the construction of a new Anhui would not be too far off. He asked for forgiveness for the inadequate hospitality and wished everyone a safe journey.

Construction of Anhui: Liu Yiyan, Director of the Construction Department of Anhui Province, reported on the construction undertakings of Anhui Province. He stated that the dikes built by the National Flood Relief Association in Anhui Province were particularly related to the future of Anhui's construction. Anhui's construction was very rudimentary and far behind Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and other provinces. The biggest reason for this was the intertwined threat of bandits and floods. Last year's floods caused rural decline and economic bankruptcy, making disaster relief a priority, let alone construction. Fortunately, with the assistance of friendly countries, the great dike project was completed. The inland river project was also successfully completed with the assistance of the Flood Relief Association. As a result, a bumper harvest was achieved this year, allowing for surplus resources to be used for construction. This should be especially thanked. He was deeply honored that prominent figures from home and abroad had come to inspect the completed dike project. He stated that the construction projects could not be fully described in a few words, and that printed materials had been prepared for reference and guidance. The main points were: 1. Transportation: Anhui Province originally had more than a thousand miles of highways, but they had been poorly maintained for many years and had not been paved with stone slabs. The projects were hastily done, and the bridges were also old. Efforts were now being made to repair them so that they could become formal highways. The sections that had been opened to traffic included the Anhe Road (Anqing to Hefei), the Hebang Road (Hefei to Bengbu), and the Wutun Road. The sections under construction included the Jingwu Road, which was expected to be open to traffic in about a month, and the Wuchang Road, which was expected to be open to traffic in about two months. 2. Water Conservancy: The principle of promoting water conservancy projects by using local resources as much as possible was adopted. Attention should be paid to repairing dikes, dredging ditches, and managing ponds so that the completed dike project could be maintained permanently. As for the administrative organization of water conservancy, the Construction Department had water conservancy engineering committees in each county, sub-committees in each district under the county, and dike engineering committees in each dike under the district. Other aspects such as forestry, mining, and tea were all being actively planned for development and improvement.

Li Zushen delivered a reply, followed by a speech by Dr. Bai Shuren, President of the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association, who stated that Vice Chairman Simpson was feeling slightly unwell and had disembarked in Wuhu to rest in the hospital before heading to Hankou to join the team. He was deeply sorry that he could not participate in tonight's grand gathering. He apologized to the Chairman on behalf of Vice Chairman Simpson. Li Zushen then delivered a thank-you speech on behalf of the Flood Relief Association, stating that he was deeply grateful for the grand hospitality of Chairman Wu of the Anhui Provincial Government and the county chiefs and committee members. He had heard that everyone had been waiting at the pier since 2:00 PM, which made him feel very sorry. At that time, his colleagues had witnessed the collapse of the Ma Jiawo riverbank and had temporarily stopped the ship to conduct an on-site inspection, as they had to personally study the protection of the dike project carefully. The round trip took a long time and delayed the schedule, so he apologized to everyone and asked for forgiveness. Li also reported on the establishment of the Flood Relief Association, concluding that the greatest contribution to the completion of the dike project was the millions of disaster relief workers. Xu Shiying and Zhou Xiangxian also delivered speeches. The party ended at 10:00 PM, and the team returned to the ship. The Jiangxin ship set sail at 10:30 PM and arrived at the mouth of the Huayang River at 2:30 AM on December 1.

Ma Hua Dike Project: At 8:00 AM, the entire team took the Anjie small boat specially prepared by the Anhui Provincial Government to Huayang Town to inspect the Ma Hua Dike. Liu Yiyan, Director of the Anhui Construction Department, also accompanied the team. The small boat sailed into the Huayang River, which was turbulent and winding. It took several miles to reach Huayang Town. The first stop was the opposite bank of Huayang Town to inspect the starting point of the Ma Hua Dike. The Ma Hua Dike was also an important dike project. Its territory was located in the three provinces of Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei, and directly affected seven counties. In terms of terrain, it was not of great importance, but its location in the three provinces made it important. It was reported that the Flood Relief Association had originally planned to abandon it, but it started construction at the request of local people. At that time, it was most difficult to hire workers because the authorities of the three provinces were unwilling to take responsibility in this no man's land. Various methods were used to barely complete the project. The dike was 9 meters wide and more than 50 kilometers long. The mud was solid, and the project was very strong, making it suitable for highway traffic. However, according to Mr. Xi Dejiong, the dike was twice as wide as ordinary dikes, and there was no need to widen it in terms of terrain, which was not in line with economic principles. Farmers also built houses on the dike, which hindered traffic. The local authorities should pay attention to this. The team then went to the opposite bank of Huayang Town to inspect the Ma Hua Dike and the location where local people planned to build a sluice gate. At 10:30 AM, the team returned to the Jiangxin ship, which sailed from Huayang, marking the end of the inspection work in the third district.

Inspection of Huikou: At 12:30 PM, the team arrived in Pengze. Local gentry boarded the ship to welcome the team. Pengze was surrounded by mountains on three sides, and houses were built against the mountains in a neat row, making for a beautiful scenery. After stopping for about ten minutes, the ship sailed again. County Chief Jiang Ji of Jiujiang County, Jiangxi Province, boarded the ship in a small boat to welcome the team. At 3:30 PM, the team arrived in Huikou. The team took the Lihu small boat to the north bank to inspect the Huikou Dike. County Chief Jiang Ji of Jiujiang County also accompanied the team. After landing, the team walked about a mile to reach the new dike. The dike was about 5 meters wide and 9.5 kilometers long, extending from Lao Zhou Tou on the Anhui border in the east to Wuxue in the west. The old dike near the river had collapsed. There were about a hundred households and some shops, making it a relatively lively village about 60 miles from Jiujiang. The Huikou Dike belonged to the fourth district project, but because it was completely contracted by the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association, it became a special district managed by the Jiujiang Chinese and Foreign Relief Association. Any matters should be reported to the Shanghai General Association. The inspection ended at 4:30 PM, and the team returned to the large ship, which sailed again. The team then went to inspect Duanyao at 5:30 PM.

Inspection of Duanyao Dike: Duanyao Town belonged to Huangmei County, Hubei Province, and was part of the fourth district dike project contracted by the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association. It connected Jiujiang in the west and Huikou in the east. The team disembarked in a small boat. County Chief Gui Fucang of Huangmei County and local gentry were already waiting at the riverbank. They accompanied the team for about two miles to reach the Duanyao Dike. The dike was 4 meters wide and about 11.5 kilometers long. As dusk was approaching, the team conducted a brief inspection and returned to the riverbank. County Chief Gui welcomed the team to the Zhao Deng Suo (recruitment and waiting place) by the river, which was used as a warehouse. The rooms were full of welcome slogans, and tea and snacks were prepared. County Chief Gui delivered a welcome speech and reported on the Duanyao Dike, stating that there were still three gaps in the Duanyao Dike that had not been repaired: 1. 2.5 kilometers long. 2. 1.5 kilometers long. 3. 1 kilometer long. The estimated cost of repairing the dike was 20,000 yuan, which was being requested from the Flood Relief Association by the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association. He then represented the people of the county in asking the Flood Relief Association not to move the dike back to avoid approaching the river channel behind it. The county government would do its best to protect the new dike. It was reported that the Flood Relief Association was very dissatisfied with the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association's request for funds. The team returned to the ship at 7:00 PM, and the Jiangxin ship sailed directly to Jiujiang.

A small part of the dikes in the fourth and fifth districts of the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association, totaling 133.7 kilometers in length, was contracted by the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association. The area on the south bank of the Yangtze River from Jiujiang to Wuxue and the north bank from Lao Zhou Tou Town to Wuxue (including the Huikou Dike) belonged to the fourth district: 1. Jiujiang to Shizi Mountain Dike: 33.5 kilometers long. 2. Lao Zhou Tou to Chen Jiaying Dike: 28.4 kilometers long. The area in the fifth district included: 1. Chen Jiaying to Xiao Chi Kou: 32 kilometers long. 2. Xiao Chi Kou to Wuxue: 42 kilometers long. The Flood Relief Association issued a total of 5,318.8 tons of wheat and grain to the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association, and the salaries of the staff and all miscellaneous expenses were paid by the Relief Association, totaling more than 90,000 yuan. Of the total length of 133 kilometers of dikes, 23 kilometers were newly built, 81 kilometers were repaired, and the rest were slightly repaired. This area was essentially a special district directly under the jurisdiction of the Shanghai General Association of the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association. (From Qian Hua in Jiujiang on December 1)

Record of the Joint Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees of the Lawyers Association 107

▲ Twenty-nine Lawyers Expelled for Unpaid Fees

The Shanghai Lawyers Association convened its 125th joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees at 10:00 AM yesterday (Sunday) at its clubhouse at the intersection of Beile Road and Lafayette Road in the French Concession. Committee members Shi, Zhu Fuju, Zhang Zhengxue, Tang Hao, Shi Liang, Yan Yinwu, Jiang Jiemin, Zhou Shiying, Shen Junru, Li Shirui, Lu Dingkui, and others were present. A letter from the Shanghai All-Circles Patriotic Volunteers Assistance Committee requesting the association to assist the arrested volunteers Liu Chongwu and others (Resolution): Referred to the Standing Committee for handling. 2. Member Zhao Zuwei's letter reporting that the Shanghai Local Court refused to accept judicial documents sold by the Special Zone Court, requesting that the association send a letter to the court requesting that it accept them as usual (Resolution): A letter was sent to the Shanghai Local Court requesting that it accept them as usual. 3. Nanjing Road Citizens Association Sends Letter Urging Members to Pay Old Price Telephone Bills 108

The Nanjing Road Businessmen's Federation and the Citizens' First District Branch, in order to accept the wishes of the majority of its members, is sparing no effort to oppose the telephone rate increase and is still actively handling the matter. However, before the negotiation is resolved, users should have the obligation to pay at the old price to avoid giving the telephone company an excuse. Therefore, a notice was issued to all members yesterday that all telephone users should immediately send a letter with a bank check attached (the check must clearly state "Pay Shanghai Telephone Company" and the words "to bearer" should be crossed out to ensure authenticity) to the company for a stamped receipt. If the company refuses to accept it, it can be sent by registered mail through the post office. The User Association and the Businessmen's Federation have sample forms attached to the payment letters. If users are still unclear about the procedures, they can inquire at the association.

Zhenhai Electric Light Company Promoters Meeting 109

▲ Resolution that the Company will not be Established

▲ And Schedule for Power Outage Set

The Zhenhai Electric Light Co., Ltd. convened a general meeting of all promoters and shareholders yesterday afternoon at the Ningbo Fellow Townsmen Association in the city. Dozens of people including Fu Xiaoan, Xu Shengchan, and Zhu Zikui attended. Chairman Wu Yaqin reported that the previously established company had been losing money and accumulating debt for many years because some influential users refused to pay the electricity bills in full and arbitrarily discounted them, making it impossible to maintain operations. In order to ensure public use, he accepted the takeover and continued to generate electricity, while actively soliciting shares and notifying users to cancel discounts and pay in full, and prohibiting electricity theft. However, his words were not heeded. As a result, the company's income did not improve, potential shareholders were hesitant to invest, and existing shareholders were unwilling to pay and questioned the situation. In this situation, not only was there no hope for the company to be formally established, but it was also feared that power generation could not be maintained. Then, Manager Yu reported on the business situation and the collection of fees, stating that the total number of users who refused to pay in full reached more than 1,000 yuan per day, resulting in significant losses. Subsequently, shareholders Qian Zhongdao, Yu Shouchun, and Liu Wanqing, and promoters Zhu Nanzhou and Dai Chengzhi, successively expressed their opinions, unanimously advocating for the dissolution of the company and the suspension of power generation. The following resolutions were passed by the entire body: 1. It was decided that the company would not be established and the preparatory office would be dissolved. 2. It was decided that power generation would be suspended starting from the 16th of this month. 3. A report on the resolution not to establish the company and the date of power suspension would be submitted to the Zhejiang Construction Department and the Zhenhai County Government for the record. 4. Notices would be sent to all users to inform them. 5. A public announcement would be made in the newspaper to inform the public. The meeting adjourned after the resolutions were passed.

Relief for Refugees in Northeast China

Their cries of sorrow are unbearable to hear. Now that winter has arrived, the north is extremely cold. The Northeast disaster victims are again crying out in the wind and snow. Eighth Anniversary of Chizhi College 113

Chizhi College, located on Shuidaidian Road in this city, had all its school buildings destroyed by the violent Japanese artillery fire during the January 28th Incident last year. This semester, thanks to the painstaking efforts of the college's president, Dr. He Shizhen, the school buildings have been rebuilt, restoring the original state. Amidst the chaos, it resolutely moved back, and the atmosphere is fresh and new. The day before yesterday (the 2nd) was the eighth anniversary of the college's founding. At 10:00 a.m., a memorial ceremony was held in the college's auditorium. All teachers, students, and guests attended the meeting. President He Shizhen reported on the history of the school's founding and delivered an encouraging speech, roughly stating that the school has experienced several major setbacks since its founding, but has managed to succeed because of its indomitable spirit and endurance. Young people should take this as a model, etc. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 p.m. At 3:00 p.m., the student union held a carnival. Although it was drizzling, over a thousand guests still arrived. The traffic on Shuidaidian Road was bustling and lively.

Obstetrics and Gynecology Specialist Qu Shaoheng and His Wife's Hospital Moves to Shanghai 114

Mr. Qu Shaoheng graduated from Osaka Medical University in Japan. He returned to China in 1916 and founded the Qu Family Hospital with his wife, Ms. Yao Yingnai, in Beijing. He used his years of academic knowledge to bring happiness to the local people. Before long, his reputation grew. In 1922, the Ministry of Education planned to send specialists to Europe, to countries like Sweden, to study medicine. Knowing that Mr. Qu had rich experience and knowledge, he was immediately appointed as a medical research specialist. He spent three years in Europe. In 1924, he returned to China. Seeing the lack of obstetrical facilities in the country, he established an obstetrical hospital in Beijing and opened a women's obstetrical school, personally taking on teaching duties. To this day, many graduates have served in society, so all circles in the former capital respect and praise Mr. and Mrs. Qu. From this, it can be seen that Mr. and Mrs. Qu have done much for the benefit of the people in the medical field during their 17 years in Beijing. Now, it is known that Mr. and Mrs. Qu have recently moved south to Shanghai because their relatives and friends in Shanghai longed for their return. At the same time, his elder brother, Mr. Shao Yi, felt deeply regretful that his younger brother had lived in the north for so long and had not been able to fulfill his duty to the poor and sick in his hometown. Therefore, he repeatedly urged them by telegram to return south to establish a hospital for consultation, so that the poor and those unable to afford medical treatment could have the opportunity for examination. Mr. Qu was deeply moved by the telegram and resolutely left Beijing and moved the Qu Family Hospital to Shanghai on the 28th of last month. They arrived in Shanghai on the 30th of last month. The hospital is now located at Nos. 32 to 34 Ningbo Road, Dongxinqiao Street, French Concession, behind the Ningbo Guild Hall. Outpatient services are available from 8:00 a.m. to 2:00 p.m. every day. House calls are available after 2:00 p.m. for temporary emergencies. Mr. and Mrs. Qu have the heart of benevolent doctors, so they do not charge the poor for consultations. This is also a ray of light for the medical community and a blessing for patients.

Large-Scale Smuggling Agencies and Distribution Centers are Established 119

Selling Opium is Very Cautious

Often Sends Followers to Secretly Follow Opium Buyers

Police Raided Two Distribution Centers

Each Sentenced to Six Months and Fined 300 Yuan

A Chaozhou Guangchang Company is a large opium trafficking agency. It has established many distribution centers in the Public Concession, which are very secret, and the police authorities have no way to investigate. A few days ago, detectives from the Narcotics Division learned that opium was sold at No. 584 Zhoujiazui Road and an unmarked bungalow on Zhaofeng Road. They sent people with money to buy it and found that it was true. They then went to the two places with Detective Chief Bai Po to arrest two Cantonese, Mei Guilin, and Ningbo, Wang Jisheng. They confiscated 29 taels of opium, a large bag of opium ash, scales, scissors, ledgers, and more than ten yuan in foreign currency. They were taken to the Huishan Police Station for detention and sent to the Third Criminal Division of the First Special District Court the next morning. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, stated the facts of the case and said that the head office, Guangchang, was large and difficult to arrest. The distribution centers were very cautious in selling opium. Whenever someone came to buy opium, they would observe the person's appearance and clothing and send followers in cars to secretly follow them to see if they were sent by the police. Therefore, he requested a severe punishment. After submitting the opium and other evidence, the Chinese and Western detectives reported the progress of the case and questioned the two defendants, whose statements were evasive. After detailed interrogation by the court, they admitted that the principal offender was Cantonese Yang Weiyi, who had already fled. They begged for leniency. Judge Shen Bingrong reviewed the confession and made a clear judgment, sentencing the defendants Mei Guilin and Wang Jisheng to six months of imprisonment each for helping to sell opium, and fining them 300 yuan each. If the fine is not paid after compulsory execution, it will be commuted to one day of imprisonment for every two yuan. The number of days detained before the judgment is determined shall be deducted from the sentence at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. The opium and other items shall be confiscated according to the list.

Reader's Consultant

Mr. He Liqing's Message December 4th 120

│See the letter from Ms. Zhang Qiuyun, December 21st│

I believe that love between husband and wife is mostly built on "spirit"│shared interests and learning. In other words: the union of husband and wife must take "spiritual" beauty as the primary condition. If the two sides have conflicting interests and cannot have equivalent learning, then no matter how talented and beautiful you are, love cannot last forever.

The current society has created the phenomenon that Ms. Yun Qiuyun described as "the love of newlyweds changes from concentrated to diluted, and then to: : : tragedy," because most people only pursue "flesh"—appearance—when choosing a partner, and ignore or even completely abandon the pursuit of "spirit."

"Flesh" has some influence on the love between husband and wife, and I cannot deny this; especially during the honeymoon period, the love between husband and wife almost entirely starts from "flesh." It would be desirable if the love between husband and wife could be as strong and sweet as during the honeymoon; however, facts tell me that this is absolutely impossible. For a husband and wife to grow old together and to prevent love from dropping from the boiling point to the freezing point and staging a tragic breakup, one must pay attention to the "spirit" in the process of love; to be clear, one must take the other party's character and learning, compatibility of interests as the first issues before getting engaged.

Whether the love between Ms. Qiuyun and the other party is completely built on "flesh," whether her interests are compatible with the other party's, and what the other party's character and learning are like, I have no way of knowing. Of course, if one does not understand someone, one is not qualified to answer for them. However, I have two contributions that may be sufficient for the lady's reference in making her own decision:

1. If the other party's interests are compatible with her, and their character and learning are not bad, and only the love is not as strong and sweet as during the honeymoon, and more emphasis is placed on obligations, then it can be said to be natural and not a problem; the reason is that there is an obligation if there is a right, there is joy if there is suffering, and the cycle of joy and suffering is "life." The moon has dark and bright phases, and flowers bloom and fall; nature is giving us many hints.

2. If the other party's interests are completely contrary to her, and their character and learning are bad, then the only way out is divorce; otherwise, it will only increase the pain.

Reporter's Note: The discussion of this issue is not yet over, and we hope that readers will express their great opinions and discuss it enthusiastically.

Mr. Mu Ouchu's Message December 4th 121

I recently saw a letter in your newspaper's Reader Consultant column from Mr. Liu Xue asking about the Anhui Fellow Association's accusation against the Disaster Relief Committee for investigating Mianzhong et al. The second point: "If the accusation is not true, how should the false accuser be punished?" The third point: "Assuming the accusation is true, how should Cha Mianzhong et al. be punished?" Attached is the opinion of your newspaper's reporter, inviting everyone to participate in the discussion. I think that this case has already been brought to justice and should be resolved according to law. Now that this case is in legal proceedings, in order to respect the law, both the plaintiff, the defendant, and the third party should wait quietly for the court to adjudicate in accordance with the law. Anyone who is in the position of a third party should pay attention to two points:

1. Are the newspapers uniformly recording and publishing the progress of the case's legal trial and the testimonies of both parties with an objective attitude?

2. Can the court make a fair and legal judgment? And is the judge's attitude toward this case fair and impartial?

In addition, in order to cultivate the spirit of the rule of law, there seems to be no need for discussion.

Mr. Li Tianfang's Letter, December 4th 122

I am a businessman, currently working as a teacher at a certain school, with a monthly salary of about 150 yuan. However, my expenses are extremely high. Household expenses alone require at least 70 or 80 yuan each month. The biggest burden is the education of my three sons. The eldest is a sophomore at a certain university in this city, and his tuition, board, and other fees cost about 200 yuan every half year. The second is my daughter, a junior at a certain middle school in this city, which costs 150 or 160 yuan per semester. The third son is only ten years old and attending elementary school, which still costs over 100 yuan every half year. And my fourth child is already five years old and urgently needs to start school. Every semester, this huge tuition fee truly drives me crazy, like an ant on a hot pan, with no solution in sight. I thought about having my eldest son drop out and find some work, but he's only two years away from graduating, and I can't bear to have his efforts wasted. I thought about having my daughter drop out, but she cries and even goes on hunger strike when I mention it. As for the third son, he's still in elementary school, and there's even less reason to have him drop out. But this won't work, and that won't work, and I really can't afford it anymore, I can't take another step. I have served in the education field for over ten years, and I always advise people to study, but while I teach other people's children, my own children face the threat of dropping out every day. This not only makes me doubt my own profession but also makes me deeply feel the difficulty of being a responsible father and brother. I remember that a few years ago, a tailor in this city committed suicide out of shame and anger because he couldn't afford to send his children to school, using his death to apologize to his children. I also have such thoughts from time to time. However, I think, in this society, there must be countless people in situations like mine. This is truly a very serious social problem. Sir, how should this problem be solved? Please submit it for everyone's discussion.

### Dance Hall Queen Wang Yuezhen Sues Lover for Seduction 123

Lived Together for Six Months, Now Suddenly Parted

If I Had Known Today, I Wouldn't Have Done It Then

Wang Yuezhen, a nineteen-year-old girl from Huai'an, Jiangsu, with a beautiful appearance, lives at No. 10 Shendeli, Baker Road. She works as a dance hostess at the Great Shanghai Dance Hall. In April of this year, she suddenly had a physical relationship with a dance patron from Guangdong, Ke Gongjie, and then began living together as lovers. Ke rented No. 18 Le'an Lane, Avenue Joffre, in the French Concession as a place to hide his mistress. It has been about six months now, and a rift suddenly appeared in their relationship, leading them to extremes. Ms. Wang, together with her father, Wang Yao'san, hired lawyer Wu Chengyu to file a criminal complaint with the First Special Court, accusing Ke of offenses such as marriage fraud and seduction. The main points of the accusation are as follows:

Wang Yuezhen, the plaintiff, is only nineteen years old and quite lovely. Due to living problems, she works as a dance hostess at the Great Shanghai Dance Hall. In April of this year, the defendant Ke Gongjie, seeing that the plaintiff had some looks, used fraudulent marriage methods to achieve the purpose of seduction. The plaintiff was young and ignorant and was eventually seduced away at the Great Shanghai Dance Hall and allowed to be sexually abused. Since then, she has been living with him at No. 18 Le'an Lane, Avenue Joffre, and has not returned home. The plaintiff searched everywhere for the plaintiff until November 5th, when she finally found her whereabouts and brought her back. However, while passing Avenue Edward VII, two foreigners recognized the plaintiff and said that Ke was sick and asked them to represent him in greeting and following her. Upon hearing this, the plaintiff was shocked and indignant. The plaintiff believes that the defendant not only seduced a virgin but also dared to instigate people to follow her, showing extreme disregard for the law. Now, the defendant, in order to achieve the purpose of sexual abuse, falsely claimed to be unmarried and willing to marry the plaintiff as his wife. There is no doubt that he used improper means to obtain the plaintiff's consent and thus gain the power of control. However, the location of the defendant's crime was the Great Shanghai Dance Hall, which is under the jurisdiction of your court. Therefore, I am forced to file this lawsuit, requesting that you quickly arrest the defendant, interrogate him, and punish him for the crime of seduction under Articles 257, Sections 1 and 2 of the Criminal Law to deter wrongdoing. In addition, I am filing a civil suit, requesting that the court order the defendant to compensate the plaintiff with a lifetime maintenance fee of 15,120 yuan (calculated at 30 yuan per month until the age of 60) to maintain her livelihood.

The court issued a subpoena based on the complaint. Because the defendant was ill and receiving treatment at the Sacred Heart Hospital on Ningguo Road in Yangshupu, police officer Guo Xiangyao No. 2591 from the Chinese constabulary informed the defendant through the hospital. The defendant saw that Guo's illness was extremely serious and he could not hold a pen. The doctor said that Ke Gongjie's illness was terminal and he would not live long. However, Ke勉力 signed the subpoena, but the doctor did not allow the subpoena and a copy of the complaint to be kept, fearing it would worsen his condition. Therefore, the officer returned the subpoena, etc. Yesterday afternoon, judge Wu Tingqi of the Special Court opened the Second Criminal Court for interrogation. After officer Guo reported the circumstances of the delivery of the subpoena, Judge Wu ruled that because the defendant was seriously ill and unable to appear in court to respond, the case could not proceed. He ordered a postponement until the defendant recovered from his illness.

### Large Group of Bandits in the Southwest of Shanghai Arrested 124

▲ Mostly Local Intellectuals

▲ Their Heinous Crimes Have Reached Their Limit, They Are All Apprehended

Recently, major cases of robbery, kidnapping, and extortion have occurred frequently in various towns and villages in the jurisdiction of the Second District of the Southwest, such as Tangwan and Caohang. Although the authorities have tightened their investigations after the cases, they have rarely been solved. Now, due to the arrest of the bandit Ding Botao in the case of the extortion of a huge sum of money from Pan Zhuxi and Shen Zhu'an in Caohang Town last month, who was sentenced to eight years in prison by the local court after interrogation by the Public Security Section, clues were obtained. Subsequently, under the secret instructions of Magistrate Yan, the Chief of the Public Security Section, Yao Fusheng, and Inspector Xu Yi, etc., paid attention to the investigation. Yao and others, together with detectives, thoroughly investigated the bandit situation in the area and learned the hideouts of various bandit gangs. They then quietly coordinated with the police of the British and French Concessions to arrest six bandits, Peng Jieren, Chen Zhuxin, Chen Haiqing, Chen Haishan, Zhang Zhaoxiang, Wang A'tudi, etc., at Anle Hotel, Wuding Road, and other places. Two pistols were seized and they were all escorted to the government office for detention. However, it was found that most of the bandits were local intellectuals who were the main leaders of the bandits. They also had some hidden power in the locality. They usually ran rampant in the countryside, committing all kinds of evil deeds. They knew who was rich and who had no money like the back of their hand. Those with a reputation and status did not dare to offend them for fear of being assassinated and could only avoid them from afar, so that these people became even more unscrupulous and regarded the law as nothing. In August of this year, when the bandit gang planned to rob a certain place, they encountered the Changqiao Security Corps and dared to resist arrest and open fire, but were scattered and fled. This time, their heinous crimes have reached their limit and they have all been apprehended. It is truly a case of the net of justice being wide and the people are celebrating the removal of this great scourge, otherwise, it would be difficult to live in peace. Since being escorted to the county, the bandits have been interrogated in detail day and night by Yao, the Chief of the Public Security Section. It is reported that the bandits have mostly confessed to their crimes and will soon be transferred to the court for trial. In addition to sending personnel to the British and French police to thank the detectives for their assistance, Magistrate Yan has also rewarded the personnel in charge of handling the case for their efforts.

### Shaoxing Fellow Villagers Association Solicits Members 127

▲ The First Period's Results Compared Today

The Shaoxing Seven Counties Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association held its sixth solicitation of members, with a deadline of one month, divided into three periods of ten days each, to be compared on the "5th," "15th," and "25th" of each month. ### Woman Collapses and Dies on the Road Due to Red Pill Poisoning 128

Yesterday around 11:00 AM, a woman wearing a freedom cloth cheongsam, with short hair, and about 30 years old, intended to go to a certain "red boy" den in Ruifuli, Rue Amiral de Mer, in the French Concession to take red pills. However, when she reached the back door of No. 57, Lane 6, she suddenly collapsed and died due to poisoning. After death, the woman's body was found to be yellow all over. It is said that she had to take three or four yuan worth of red pills every day when she was alive.

### Young Man Crushed to Death by a Public Bus 129

According to the Central News Agency, Cai Jionglin, a 21-year-old from Changshu, lived at No. 1055 Siwenli, Xinzhapu Road. His family was poor and his father was old. He used to be a tailor, but recently, he was unemployed at home. His mother worked as a servant to supplement the family income. His younger brother was only eight years old. A few months ago, he was introduced to work as an accountant at a certain restaurant on Caishi Road, and the family depended on him. To save on commuting expenses, he borrowed a bicycle. On the day before yesterday (2nd), at around 10:00 PM, he was riding his bicycle home from the shop. When he reached Datong Road and Xinzha Road, a No. 10 public bus, disregarding traffic rules, did not stop at the station and drove straight on. He shouted for the bus to stop, but he had already been hit and killed. The next day, his parents were very worried because their son had not returned home all night, but they thought he might have stayed at the shop due to the rain. When they heard rumors from neighbors, they went out to inquire. Yan Wenhan, a clerk from Yuan Tai Xiang, explained that he had witnessed everything and was willing to testify. Knowing that the deceased was their son, the old mother and young brother suffered a great blow and were in extreme grief. The scene was unbearable to witness. The public bus company should show humanitarian consideration and provide generous compensation. It is reported that the court will open a trial on this matter within days.

### Girl Crushed to Death by a Train 130

Xiao Sanzi, a nine-year-old girl, the daughter of Gu Wenbao, a Yancheng native living near the Da Yang Bridge in Zhabei, was playing by the railway near the Da Yang Bridge at around 10:00 AM yesterday when a Shanghai-bound Jinghu train passed by and knocked Xiao Sanzi down, crushing her head and killing her instantly. The road police arrived and notified Gu Wenbao and ordered the local guarantor Zhang Fengqi to report to the local court for an autopsy.

International Race Walking, Chinese Team Wins for the Fifth Consecutive Year 137

England Second, One Point Behind

France Third::: Ireland Fourth

Italy Fifth::: Russia Sixth

Shi Jinsheng Creates New Record

Two Hours, Twenty-Three Minutes, Forty Seconds

The national race walking team won its fifth consecutive championship in the International Race Walking competition, to the cheers of hundreds of thousands of people in Shanghai yesterday, maintaining its championship and defeating England, Ireland, France, Italy, and Russia. Shi Jinsheng retained his individual title and created a new record with a time of two hours, twenty-three minutes, and forty seconds, breaking his previous record of two hours, twenty-seven minutes, and three seconds from the previous competition. The English team, despite its best efforts, finished second with twenty-one points, just one point behind. France finished third with fifty-three points, Ireland fourth with fifty-four points, Italy fifth with sixty-six points, and Russia sixth because one of its representatives arrived after the allotted time and had no points.

Victory Celebration Banquet 142

Southeast Wins the Group B Championship of the China Women's Basketball League 146

Yesterday evening, won against Chongde with a score of 29 to 16.

The triangular finals of the Group B of the China Women's Basketball Association saw the Southeast and Chongde teams eliminate Xiaguang one after another. Yesterday afternoon at 5:30 PM, the two teams held the final match at the China Basketball Hall. The Southeast B team ultimately defeated Chongde, avenging their previous defeat, and the championship was won by Southeast. The score was 29 to 16.

At the beginning, the two teams competed fiercely, each scoring points, and the situation was tense. In the first eight minutes, Southeast took the lead by one point, with the score at 8 to 7. From the second quarter onwards, Southeast's momentum suddenly surged, becoming unstoppable. Chongde found it difficult to attack and defend, making a poor showing. Chongde only scored two points, while Southeast scored as many as nine points. Chongde suffered a major blow and found it difficult to win the championship.

In the first half, Southeast had already won with a score of 17 to 9. Their spirits were greatly boosted, their courage was strong, and their power was awe-inspiring. On the other hand, Chongde appeared timid and flustered, getting worse and worse. By the end of the third quarter, Southeast was leading with a score of 25 to 11. In the last eight minutes, the situation between the two sides became tense again. Chongde tried hard to retaliate, but their excessive point deficit led to failure. In the end, they willingly admitted defeat, and the championship was won by Southeast. The results are as follows:

Ministry of Education Explains the Solicitation of Members by District Education Associations 151

The Ministry of Education, based on an inquiry from the Jiangsu Education Department regarding whether district education associations under the jurisdiction of various counties and cities can solicit members at any time, issued an instruction explaining that within the area of a district education association, those who meet the qualifications of Article 16 of the Education Association Law (Article 16 stipulates that members of the Education Association, except for students in school who cannot be members, are limited to citizens of the Republic of China over the age of 20 within the area who meet one of the following qualifications: (1) current teachers or staff members of public or registered schools or social education institutions, but accountants, clerks, and secretaries among the staff are not included; (2) current educational administrators; (3) graduates of public or registered high schools or schools with equivalent qualifications; (4) graduates of public or registered old-system middle schools or schools equivalent to old-system middle schools who have served in the field of education for more than one year; (5) those who have made definite studies of education and have works on education. The qualifications of the aforementioned members shall be determined by a member qualification review committee organized by the supervisory authority in charge) may be solicited to become members. If the legal number of members is still not met after solicitation, the provisions of Article 2 of the Implementing Rules of the Education Association Law shall be followed (Article 2 stipulates that if there are fewer than 20 members in a district and a district education association cannot be organized, they may join a neighboring district education association or jointly organize an education association with other districts).

Ministry of Education Promulgates Standards for Kindergarten and Elementary School Curriculum (40) 154

Abacus Calculation

1. Methods of moving beads.

2. Methods of positioning.

3. Practice of addition.

4. Practice of subtraction.

5. Practice of multiplication with one-digit multiplier.

6. Practice of multiplication with two-digit multiplier.

Grade 4: 60 minutes

1. Review addition.

2. Review subtraction.

3. Review multiplication.

4. Division with a one-digit divisor.

5. Methods of writing and reading numbers within 10,000.

6. Multiplication with a multiplier of three or more digits.

7. Division with a two-digit divisor.

8. Addition and subtraction of whole decimals.

9. Multiplication of whole decimals.

10. Division of whole decimals.

11. Application of four operations.

12. Jin-liang measurement system.

30

Notes

1. For written arithmetic, items 1 to 11 of the first and second grades are taught in the first academic year without using formulas, and only arithmetic knowledge is provided on a random basis, so the time is only set at 60 minutes per week. Item 12 and below are taught in the second academic year. Items 1 to 16 of the third and fourth grades can be listed in the third academic year, and items 17 and below can be listed in the fourth academic year. Items 1 to 16 of the fifth and sixth grades can be listed in the fifth academic year, and the rest can be included in the sixth academic year. Abacus calculation starts from the fourth academic year.

2. In villages or remote areas, the children in the first and second grades are older. Before entering school, they already have a lot of quantitative experience and common sense, as well as calculation habits. Therefore, it is appropriate to assign the items of the first and second grades and items 1 to 15 of the third and fourth grades in a row, and complete them in about two years.

3. If there is a need for foreign weights and measures and foreign currencies in various places, they can be appropriately increased. For example, in Qingdao, South Manchuria, etc., a comparison of the Chinese-Japanese system can be added. Other similar cases can be inferred. Those who do not need it in the mainland can be omitted.

4. Key Points of Teaching Methods

(1) The arithmetic in the first academic year should be taught randomly without specifying formal time, or it can be linked with other designs for teaching. The second academic year can be the same as the first academic year, or formal time can be specified for teaching. It is up to each school to implement it according to its own convenience.

(2) The arithmetic below the third and fourth grades should be fully linked with other designs for teaching. In the teaching time of each section, the third and fourth grades should extract 5 to 10 minutes, and the fifth and sixth grades should extract 10 minutes for independent practice of calculation skills. From the fourth grade, "Arithmetic Practice Test" should also be used.

(3) The materials in the first and second academic years should be based on daily food, clothing, and supplies. The third and fourth academic years should be based on food, clothing, housing, transportation, school assignments, and family economics. The fifth and sixth academic years should be based on economic issues such as food, clothing, housing, transportation, schools, families, society, and international relations, with special emphasis on practice in buying and selling, finding change, and discounts, but they must be used flexibly according to local conditions and children's interests.

(4) The homework in the first and second academic years must be entrusted to games, and taught using methods such as competitions, or store opening exercises. This method must also be applied frequently after the third academic year so that children work hard out of interest.

(5) The problems must be concrete and interesting. In the lower grades, the method of performance should be fully used to turn the problem into a fact so that the children can see it directly. Up to the third and fourth grades, the problem should also be made into a story to help the children imagine the facts.

(6) The writing of the problems must be clear and simple, and the content must not be convoluted so that children cannot easily understand it.

(7) New methods and principles should start from practical needs, first making children understand the usefulness of the method, and proceeding step by step using the inductive method. Avoid using the deductive method.

(8) The calculation methods for solving problems do not need to use too much theoretical analysis, but must appeal to children's experience and common sense.

(9) Mental calculation is the foundation of arithmetic and must be practiced very skillfully.

(10) Special attention should be paid to practicing the algorithm of short numbers (that is, numbers within ten) used in daily life.

(11) Written calculation and abacus calculation are both tools to help with mental calculation. Of course, schools can teach both abacus calculation, because it is more difficult to learn than written calculation in base ten because of the carry-over. When teaching, it should be fully connected with written calculation and pay attention to the familiarity of fingers.

(12) The formation of habits such as rapid calculation comes gradually and cannot be achieved overnight. Therefore, the steps should be carefully planned and applied step by step to seek progress from unfamiliarity to proficiency.

(13) The methods of practice should be varied in many ways, and the interest of children in success should be used to make them work hard.

(14) Approximate calculation and verification calculation should be paid attention to from the beginning of teaching in the lower grades.

(15) In the fifth and sixth grades, attention should be paid to the practice of four operations application problems that are needed in daily life, but the principle is to be simple.

Muslims Send Personnel Abroad to Investigate Education 158

Purpose: Emerging Countries such as Turkey and Persia

The Chinese Muslim People's Association has now sent Ma Songting, Zhang Runzhi, and Zhao Zhenwu abroad to investigate the educational conditions of emerging countries such as Turkey and Persia. Ma and others led Wang Shiming, Han Hongkui, Ma Jinpeng, Jin Diangui, Zhang Bingduo, and other students studying abroad from Beiping Chengda Normal School to Shanghai yesterday from Beijing. They also hold study abroad certificates issued by the Ministry of Education. They are now staying at the Qingzhen Temple on Zhejiang Road. Ma and others plan to send these students to Al-Azhar University in Cairo, Egypt, to study education and philosophy, as the university has a history of over a thousand years and is the oldest among European universities. After sending these students to Cairo, Ma and the other two will depart from there, pass through Arabia, and go to emerging Muslim countries such as Turkey and Persia to investigate education conditions. Then, they will return to China via Afghanistan and India. The ship has been booked and will set sail on the Italian ship Conte Rosso on the 9th of this month. Most of the Muslims in this port are preparing to see them off.
