The colleagues are not talented, but are willing to be pioneers.

Page 20

Shanghai's Architectural Undertakings Increase Day by Day 184

— Fang Fuan

▲ The Past Five Years Called the Great Era of Architecture

▲ The Prosperity of This Port Will Tend to Be More Solid in the Future

This port is located on the shore of Chun Shen, with a superior location in the country. The Huangpu River meanders for twenty-five miles to reach the sea. Since the opening of trade, it has been called the communication center of Asia and the only major port in our country. However, in the past ten years, natural and man-made disasters in the country have followed one after another, and the world economy has also had an impact. It is difficult for all industries to avoid withering, but Shanghai has been able to remain stable and its prosperity has become more solid because of the daily increase and prosperity of its architectural undertakings. The past five years have been called the greatest era of architecture in China. Last year's January 28th Incident, the prosperity of Zhabei was all reduced to ashes, but thanks to the city government's efforts to seek revival, it is not difficult to gradually restore the old appearance of the pre-war scenery. The construction of the central administrative district of the city will also be completed in the near future. Recalling when the Battle of Shanghai was in full swing and the sound of artillery was deafening, many of the construction workers in this port were joyfully busy with the work of transporting sand, steel, and wood. The sound of hammering and the sound of artillery echoed each other, and the architectural fever at sea was like this, which is quite amazing. The statistical report on the construction of this port this year has not yet been completed, but the fact that it is rising steadily and has no end is undeniable. The amount spent on new buildings in this port was 45 million taels of silver in 1929, 70 million taels of silver in 1930, and slightly less due to the Shanghai Incident in 1931, dropping to 60 million taels of silver. As for this year's expenses, it is estimated by the general public to be around 60 million taels of silver. Now, I will briefly describe the content and situation of some of the buildings that have been completed or are under construction in this port, in order to see the general situation of the major buildings in this port.

Twenty-Two-Story Building of the Four Banks

㈠ Twenty-Two-Story Building of the Four Banks

Designed by Architect Udalak

Constructed by Fu Ji Construction Factory

The twenty-two-story building of the Four Banks Savings Association currently under construction can be called the tallest building at sea, and also the tallest building in the Eastern Hemisphere. It was designed by architect Udalak in this port. The foundation of the new building is located at the corner of Jing'an Temple Road and Park Road, facing the racecourse, covering an area of approximately 3,000 square feet. The engineer and contractor of the foundation is Kangyi Foreign Firm. The entire new building is constructed with a full steel frame, and the steel materials are supplied by Siemens China Company, representing the Wanhua steel factory (American steel factory). This steel material is a kind of gold-containing manganese steel, and its outstanding advantages include the following: high yield, high ductility, excellent rust prevention, and extremely satisfactory use. The tensile strength of the steel frame is 35.5 to 42 tons per square inch, or 52 kg per square meter, which is much higher than the 37 kg per square meter tensile strength of the steel materials used before. After the new building is completed, the ground floor, the first floor, and the basement will be used as the new site of the Four Banks Savings Association. The bank hall will be located on the ground floor, and the offices will be located on the first floor. As for the great vault and 6,000 safe deposit boxes, they will be installed in the basement. From the second floor to the twenty-second floor, it will be completely used for private residences and apartment hotels. The dining room is located on the second floor, and there is a public rest area on the fourteenth floor, facing the roof garden. The cost of the new building is a total of 2 million taels of silver, and it is being constructed by Fu Ji Construction Factory, founded by Mr. Tao Guilin. (To be continued)

The left picture shows the planned building located on the empty ground opposite the Hamilton Building at the corner of Jiangxi Road and Simal Road. The name and use of the building will be reported later. 185

— Shen Tong

Architecture and History 186

— Liu Futai

Historians do not always write history in books, because books are easily destroyed. If it is written on buildings, it can be preserved for a long time and is not easily destroyed. We can learn more and more truthfully about the work of ancient humans from the surviving remains than from handwriting. Can we now write our history on buildings, hoping it will last as long as our Great Wall of China and the Egyptian pyramids?

It is hoped that people today can imagine themselves as future archaeologists, excavating the surviving remains of modern buildings. This archaeologist can obtain the most interesting and novel information about the lives of modern people, which can give him the most peculiar and amazing feeling. Sometimes they will definitely go to see the existing buildings, monuments, and ruins of cities, and use a critical eye. After seeing them, they will know that these buildings were originally built for work, and the roads were built for cars. Their interest will immediately turn from private to public. In short, in this way, we can see our entire history. Because this kind of history is not like the historical narratives written in words by historians with personal opinions or creators of myths, such as some emotional narratives in Sima Qian's "Historical Records" and the myth of Pangu creating the world. However, this kind of architectural history is permanent, true, and unbiased. Architects are truly sincere historians, and their records are true and free of prejudice. They must be commanded and governed by the environment of the times, and they cannot arbitrarily prove the needs of industry and the demands of the people. Therefore, architects are people who leave behind true records. Try to imagine finding two architectural historians from the same era, just like two buildings of the same model. That is the result of their records.

Ordinary historians' records of history are inevitably based on personal observations, but after a long period of time, their records are regarded as true facts, and thus the personal basis of the situation is lost. However, architects will never have this kind of change. Architects' construction is based on the requirements of the environment and the urgency of the times, so this kind of record remains until the building is destroyed.

Important Tasks of Today's Architectural Circle 187

— Tan Zidian, Shanghai Architectural Association

Urgent Need to Open an Eastern Major Port

The architectural industry is of great importance to the rise and fall of a country. It is also closely related to human happiness. The development of the architectural industry in European and American countries is growing day by day. Publications on architectural studies fill bookstores. Looking back at our country, specialized writings and periodicals on architectural studies are as rare as phoenix feathers and unicorn horns, and cannot be seen much. The Shen Bao authorities, aware of this, have compiled a "Special Architectural Issue." The Shen Bao editors came to the association to meet with Mr. Du Yangeng, the standing committee member of the association, and discussed in detail the issue of improving the architectural industry. Mr. Du told them the tasks of today's architectural circle. In a nutshell, he said that we must start from practical work. For the sake of the development of national industry and the progress of the entire architectural circle, we must not delay. He elaborated on his various plans, and I recorded them as follows.

Domestic architectural publications are already extremely rare, but if one investigates their content, they are full of empty talk and make no concrete contributions to the development of national industry or the practical work of the architectural circle. What I hope for from the "Special Architectural Issue" is that it can eliminate common mistakes and guide the architectural circle with practical work, so as not to fail the original intention of publication.

Opening commercial ports is the most important and significant mission undertaken by the architectural circle in recent times. The late Premier, in his industrial plan for nation-building, had already elucidated the plan to open the three major ports in the East, North, and South. The realization of this plan depends on our colleagues in the architectural circle and those who aspire to engage in the architectural industry. We should work hard to promote its realization so that we can complete the plan of the late Premier. The initial progress should start with the opening of the Eastern Major Port, and then extend to the opening of the Northern Major Port and the Southern Major Port. It is also hoped that the people of the country can invest in it.

Opening up the Eastern Major Port

The Eastern Major Port is located in Hangzhou Bay, between Zhapu Cape and Ganpu Cape. Its location and transportation are superior. Once it is opened and developed, who knows that today's barrenness will not become the only bustling market in the East in the future, comparable to New York in the United States and London in England. A hundred years ago, who could have foreseen the prosperity of New York and London today? Regarding the opening of the Eastern Major Port, the late Premier had a detailed plan. Now I quote his words: "The distance from Zhapu Cape to Ganpu Cape is about fifteen miles. A seawall should be built from this cape to that cape, and a gap should be opened at the Zhapu end a few hundred feet away from the mountain as the main entrance to the port. This kind of seawall can be divided into five sections, each three miles long. Because now we build one section first, three miles long and one and a half miles wide, we will get a port area of three or four square miles, which is enough for use. (To be continued)

A Brief Biography of Architect Zhuang Jun 188

Architect Zhuang Jun, courtesy name Daqing, is a native of Shanghai, 45 years old. He graduated from Nanyang Middle School and studied at Xujiahui Nanyang University and Tangshan Railway and Mining School. Then, he passed the examination for the second session of the US Study Affairs Office and entered the University of Illinois in the United States to study architecture. In the third year of the Republic of China, he returned to China after completing his studies and served as the resident architect of Tsinghua University in Beiping, serving for nine years. In the twelfth year of the Republic of China, he traveled to the United States again and entered Columbia University. In the fourteenth year, he traveled to various European countries. After returning to China, he established an office in Shanghai, specializing in architectural design and supervision. The new buildings of Jin Cheng, Jiao Tong, Da Lu, and other banks in Shanghai, Hankou, Jinan, Qingdao, Harbin, Dalian, Nanjing, and other ports were all planned by him alone. The Da Lu Shopping Mall in this city is also one of his recent carefully crafted works. In the eighteenth year of the Republic of China, he was registered as an industrial technician by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the National Government, a member of the Chinese Institute of Engineers, and served as the president, vice president, director, and consultant of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the National Government.

Film Special Issue

Monday, December 5, Year 21 of the Republic of China

No Extra Charge

Opinions and Contributions

The Need for More Short Films 190

— Xin

It's strange that many people only pay attention to the feature film when watching a movie, as if the short film is insignificant. This is a huge mistake! I'm afraid this is the main reason why the Chinese film industry ignores short films.

The currently popular short films are nothing more than the following: 1. News; 2. Comedy; 3. Song and dance; 4. Children's plays or dog plays; 5. Charcoal drawings; 6. Science; 7. Scenery; 8. Others!

If we look for them in domestic films, the total number of short films is less than twenty. Of course, short films are just as troublesome to produce as feature films, and they don't sell for much money. Therefore, except for sensational news, such as sports competitions, almost no one is willing to spend effort and money to produce them. The lack of short films has led to the current depression of domestic films, and adding foreign short films before showing domestic films (mostly silent films) is inevitably incongruous. Therefore, we have to lengthen domestic films, sometimes meaningless, or simply shorten them in a simple way so that they must be about 11,000 feet long, enough for an hour and forty-five minutes of screening. There is no flexibility, which is an extremely far-fetched and difficult thing.

In the current situation, when there is a lack of film talents in China, shooting short films that do not require actors or that practice new actors is not a difficult task. For example, in the news aspect: great people flying around, the construction of various industries, grand ceremonies. There is no day without them: there are many good materials, which will definitely arouse the interest of the audience. In terms of scenery, China has great ancient architecture: there are different customs in North China and South China: the lives of Mongolia, Xinjiang, and Yunnan-Guizhou; which one is not what we like to see? Moreover, the natural beauty of the north and south of the Yangtze River is inexhaustible. Speaking of song and dance films: it is also possible to shoot some Chinese stage plays, which can not only adjust the tastes of the audience, but also be good cultural propaganda products if they are sold to foreign countries. It is more effective and lasting than Dr. Mei going to the United States. Isn't China trying to shoot comedy films? We should start with short film auditions, otherwise there will be no good results. Who among Rock, Chaplin, and Laurel and Hardy was not honed in short films? ·········

To give another example, ten years ago, MGM produced very few feature films, and all its energy was put on short films. What about now? Its position surpasses any film studio. Of course, the credit of short films is very large, and even this year, the average number of short films is still twice that of feature films. This is a good model and a good policy for film studios!

If you think that short films are not popular, that is a fact that can be proved. For example, the most monotonous landscape film, if it can be photographed skillfully and matched with high mountains and flowing water songs or music, how artistic is it? How can it be dry?

"Everything depends on human effort." If you want domestic films to develop and work for art: then you should focus on small things and start with exquisitely produced short films!

Two black-clad girls, who do you think they are?

They are Chen Yumei (right) and Li Minghui (left): both are pillars of Tianyi Company.

Celebrities Should Also Be Tailors 191

— Meng Hu

GillbirlAdiain now has a good business acumen, that is, to be the designer of the costumes of MGM's actresses. He is indeed a talented art expert. The strange Javanese and Russian costumes in Garbo's "Camille" added a lot of charm to Garbo. This is a good example of his talent.

Film Review

Review of "Little Actress" 192

— Xiang Shi

What is most difficult for a screenwriter is that when starting to write a script, he wants to write a script with a sound consciousness, but when the entire script is completed, for the sake of plot, structure, interspersion, etc., the original consciousness will often disappear by more than half. When the film is made, if the performance is not strong enough, or even makes the original consciousness only a trace.

If you want to find a bit of consciousness in the script of "Little Actress," there are only some vague shadows of "benevolence" and "filial piety." I speculate that the original intention of the screenwriter was to make a deeply touching ethical drama, but there are too many negative descriptions, which shift the audience's attention to the negative descriptions, making it overwhelm the positive.

From the perspective of the whole story, the first half describes the decline of an old family, and the second half describes the suffering of a shrew and a rogue. From beginning to end, a naive little girl is used as a connection, and the structure is quite good. Some people think that the description of Wang's shrewishness and Chen Naixin's viciousness is a bit too much, but I think there are extremely vicious people in the world, but we rarely encounter them.

The director has several very clever places, such as Wang's smashing of the photo frame sent by Ji Zhong, interspersed with Ji Zhong crying on the ground in the kitchen.

Also, Wang and Chen Naixin beat each other, transforming into Zhang Xiaolin and another little actress practicing gun skills, and the movements and postures are similar. These kinds of shots are both reasonable and interesting. As for the close-up of the wheels of the car when Wang and Naixin went to the racecourse, and the close-up of the wheels of the audience when the pastoral volume was shown, the repeated use of it seems to be meaningless.

The performance is best by the protagonist Yuan Meiyun. Some people say that she was originally a little actress, and now she plays a little actress on the screen, which is naturally very suitable. This seems reasonable, but it is not true, because the performance in drama films is different from real life. For example, if there is an officer, he is asked to play an officer on the stage or in the film, he may not perform well. Therefore, Yuan Meiyun's success in "Little Actress" is that she does have the talent for performance, and does not rely on her life experience, because her life process will never have the experience of joys and sorrows in the "Little Actress" drama.

The performances of other actors are all on the horizontal line. Shu Lijuan's shrew and Ge Furong's coward have more opportunities to perform, but they can only arouse the audience's superficial laughter and cannot make the audience get a deep impression.

The light and scenery are all good, and the sound is also very clear, but it is a pity that there are a few places with a little noise, which is a bit imperfect!

Common Myopia 193

— Yun

At present, everyone's understanding of a film actor, whether male or female! Especially female actors, is inevitably superficial, and does not actually pursue their success or failure. I think this is very dangerous.

Is this actor's face beautiful? Is she a passionate girl? Or is his or her dress fashionable or not? This has almost become a common meal for ordinary people to criticize a film actor.

In fact, this is really a huge mistake.

Who is a successful actor? I think only by criticizing with the standard of "how superb is his or her art" is correct. Film is an art "this is known to everyone, so a film is definitely not successful by relying on a few beautiful faces or some superficial expressions. The art of actors' performance is its only life element.

Therefore, the success of an actor is undoubtedly not able to be promoted by those people's superficial criticism. It is pitiful, is the common people's myopia.

Opinion Announcement

More Attention Should Be Paid to the Cultivation of Child Actors 195

— Jinsha

A family without children feels boring; at the same time, the movie would be too monotonous if there were no children.

In domestic films, it can simply be said that there are no child actors, which really makes us extremely disappointed.

In fact, the performance ability of children is not lower than that of adults, and there are many places where only children can perform. Children's expressions are innocent, without affectation, without hypocrisy. Like the performance of the little friend in the humanitarianism produced by Lianhua, it really moves us. In many places, it is more touching to have children perform than adults. The little friend in "Humanity" is a good example.

Therefore, we are eager for the birth of child actors. Naturally, it is more difficult for a director to train a child actor than to train ten adults, but we hope that the director will not be afraid of difficulties. I hope that the director can put the energy of training ten adults on one child actor.

Movies are great, and children's movies are especially great! Don't forget the great responsibility! Director and film company!

Letter Disclosure 196

Dear Editor, yesterday I read several short messages published in your journal by Jizhong, which contained many inaccuracies. The most bizarre thing is that it was actually said that since Li Ping and other gentlemen joined our company, there has been a division between the old and new factions within the company, and there is a lack of cooperation in form and spirit, which may hinder the company's future. After reading it, I was extremely surprised and noticed that the intention was close to instigation. Since Li and other gentlemen have joined successively, they have been harmonious with the original employees and actors, so the work has proceeded very smoothly. The so-called division of the new and old factions is all fabrication. Although I dare not be sure whether the author intends to slander, but this kind of nonsense has appeared in the newspaper, and if it causes suspicion, it is really detrimental to our company. Therefore, I specially send a letter hoping that you will correct it on our behalf. I am very grateful and respectful to you. Xingming Film Company, twenty-one, eleven, thirty,

Editor's Note: Jizhong is one of the contributors to this journal, and the news collected may contain inaccuracies. As soon as it is published, it will damage the reputation of the other party. I am very grateful for the letter from Xingming Company pointing out this. In addition to disclosing and correcting the original letter, I also hope that Mr. Jizhong can explain it. (Not sensitive)

Local Rare News

What are the female stars doing after leaving the photography scene? (Part 1) 197

— Xingxiu

The luxury and romance of the lives of female movie stars are of course not limited to Hollywood alone, and the same is true for Chinese female stars. Here, I am only talking about a part of the lives of Chinese female stars, that is, what they do after leaving the photography scene.

Their hobbies are naturally not the same. After they have finished their serious work and left the photography scene, what they do is undoubtedly not the same.

Due to different times or climates, the work they do after completing their work also changes with the time and climate. For example, in summer, female stars go to Gaohashi beach to swim, but in winter, they will not go anymore. Now I can only write a little about what they usually and daily do.

Ruan Lingyu often plays mahjong to pass the time, but she cannot be determined to be the one who loves playing mahjong the most. Lin Chuchu is her old mahjong partner. They both work in the first factory of Lianhua. Xia Peizhen also often borrows mahjong to pass the time when she is idle. She also has an old partner who is in the same game with her, who is Hua Wanfang.

Lin Chuchu already has two children. The older one is a son and the younger one is a daughter, namely Li Keng and Li Xuan. They have both shown their faces in the film "Humanity". These two lively and lovely children are Lin Chuchu's second life. She can take care of the warmth, food, and all the responsibilities related to the health of the children, and sometimes she has to make clothes for the children, and she is a loving mother. Xu Qinfang loves her children in the same way as her. Ms. Xu originally had four children, and one died last year. Now there are still three. (To be continued)
